Kane dwen ho sɛ ɔbɛkɔ
Mihuu kommyɛ soronko bi bere a na yɛne Leeds reko wɔ dapɛn awiei no.
Harry Kane taa tu mmirika no pii sen obi foforo biara, na bere nyinaa ɔde akwankyerɛ ne akwankyerɛ ma agumadifo foforo sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛbɔ wɔn bɔ no yiye.
Ɔyɛɛ dinn wɔ Leeds ho, na ɔyɛɛ dinn sen sɛnea misusuw sɛ mahu no pɛn.
Misusuw sɛ yei yɛ sɛnkyerɛnne a ɛkyerɛ sɛ Harry adwenem yɛ no nãã wɔ ahometew a ɔwɔ wɔ Spurs no ho, na ɔrehwehwɛ ɔkwan a ɔbɛfa so afi mu dedaw.
Mpataku ho pere wɔn sɛ wɔbɛtu mmirika
Awiei koraa no, Nuno Espirito Santos agye atom sɛ wɔ mfɛnsere a wɔde tu kwan no mu no ɛsɛ sɛ ɔde ne nsa hyɛ krataa foforo ase.
Winger Pedro Neto ne ntamgyinafoɔ a wɔfrɛ wɔn Ruben Neves ne wɔn a wɔadi kan akyerɛ mmerɛwyɛ a ɛwɔ Wolves atuateɛ no mu.
Fabio Silva ne Raul Jimenez na wɔka wɔn a ɛdi hɔ a wɔakyerɛw wɔn din, nanso Jimenez ayɛ n'ade wɔ November mu bere a wɔbɔɔ ne tikora mu no.
Mpataku wɔ botae 13 a ɛnnu afe a etwaam no wɔ afe yi mu.
Wolves boayikuo no ahyɛ Nuno bɔ sɛ ɔde ne nsa bɛhyɛ obi a ɔwɔ botaeɛ ho nimdeɛ ase.
Wɔbɛka akyerɛ Jimenez wɔ Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so dunan mu sɛ ɔwɔ apɔwmuden a ɔde bedi agoru abien a etwa to wɔ afahyɛ yi mu a.
Watete no asram abien nanso wɔbaraa no sɛ ɔnni bɔɔl no anim na ɔne ne dɔm no nni nkitaho.
Owura Alex kamfo McTominay
Sɛ Owura Alex Ferguson ɔkɛseɛ no ka Manchester United ho asɛm a, ɛfata sɛ yetie no bere nyinaa.
N’ani gye Scott McTominay ho yiye, na owura no se ɛsɛ sɛ bɔɔlbɔni no ankasa bɔ wɔ United game biara mu.
Owura Alex kae sɛ: “ Scott McTominay apue sɛ United bɔɔlbɔkuo kɛseɛ no mu baako.”
“Sɛ wohwɛ United boaboa wɔn bɔɔlbɔkuo ano wɔ agodie bi a ɛho hia mu a, McTominay din wɔ mu.
Ɔwɔ suban pa na ɔtete afoforo yiye.
Bere a na ɔyɛ abofra a wadi mfe ason anaa nwɔtwe pɛ no, mede me nsa hyɛɛ ne nsa
Na ɔyɛ obi a ɔwɔ mfinimfini ankasa.”
Ayeyi a ɛkyɛn so bɛn na bɔɔlbɔni betumi anya?
Bɔɔlbɔ mu nokwasɛm ahorow mmiɛnsa a ɛyɛ nwonwa...
* Manchester United nhweree agodie biako pɛ wɔ PL no mu afe ne asram anan!
Sɛ wɔanni nkunim wɔ wɔn bɔɔlbɔ a edi hɔ no mu a, Sheffield United bɛba abɛyɛ bɔɔlbɔkuo a ɛdi kan a wɔadi nkunim wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako akyi.
Dr. Madzorera kaaɛ sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ apɔmuden adwumakuo no nso ma nkurɔfo hu yareɛ no yie, na wɔfrɛ wɔ telefon so wɔ ɔman no afanan nyinaa sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a nkurɔfoɔ bɛtumi afrɛ wɔn bere biara de aka yareɛ no ho asɛm.
Wɔrekamfo akyerɛ nso sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ahotew mu nhwehwɛmu, na ɛnyɛ sɛ wɔbɛtwɛn sɛ obi a wosusuw sɛ ɔwɔ yare mmoawa no bi bɛfa no akɔ ayaresabea.
Caps United guamtenani Lewis Uriri se wɔadi ɔhaw a wɔn bɔɔlbɔkuo no refa mu no ho dwuma na bɔɔlbɔkuo a wɔn ho yɛ hu yi ahyɛ aseɛ resiesie wɔn ho ama Castle Premier Soccer League akansi no.
Berɛ a ɔne Studi 7, rekasa no, Uriri kaa sɛ wɔmaa agodiebɔfoɔ yi sika a ɛda nsow.
Nanso ɔkae sɛ ɔsram a etwaam no wɔbɛtua bɔɔlbɔfo ka nnansa yi ara. Ɔsan nso kaa sɛ nnipa bi a wɔmmɔ wɔn din na wɔrehyɛ Caps United bɔɔlbɔfo no ma wagyae bɔɔlbɔ.
Uriri kaa sɛ ɔne bɔɔlbɔkuo no akasa, na ɔsan nso kaa nea enti a wɔtwentwɛɛ wɔn nan ase wɔ bɔɔlbɔkuo no akatua ho ne sɛ na nneɛma mu yɛ den ma obiara a ɔwɔ ɔman no mu, ɛne sɛ aban mmaa bɔɔlbɔkuo no bosea afe a etwaam no.
Wɔn a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔde wɔn ho hyɛ ɔbarima ne ɔbea nna mu no ka sɛ ehia sɛ wɔyɛ nsakrae wɔ mmara a ɛfa nyinsɛn a wotu gu ho no mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a saa bere no bɛkɔ so na abɔ mmeawa ne mmea nkwa ho ban.
Sayendisa Ndlovu a ɔfiri SayWhat se ɔmanfoɔ nnim nyinsɛn a wotu gu mmara no ho hwee, na ɔka sɛ ɛho hia sɛ aban bɔ mmara no dawuru.
Ndlovu ka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔyɛ nsakrae wɔ mmara no mu sɛnea wɔkyerɛw no tete no. Ɔkae sɛ ɛho hia sɛ wɔyɛ nsakrae wɔ mmara no mu na wɔde nneɛma foforo a ebetumi ama obi apɔn yafunu aka ho.
Ndlovu kaa sɛ nneɛma bi te sɛ adwenem yare, HIV / AIDS anaa dɛmdi ne nneɛma bi a ɛma yetumi tu nyinsɛn gu.
Ndlovu nso kyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ mmara no nnyɛ ayaresabea ahodoɔ nkutoo na ɛsɛ sɛ wotu nyinsɛn gu, na saa ara nso na ɛnhwehwɛ sɛ abofra ɔyarehwɛfo anaa dɔkota beyi obi nyinsɛn agu mmara kwan so.
Awuraa Tendaishe Changamire, a ɔko fa ɔmanfo kyɛfa ho wɔ Right Here seesei dwumadie ase no nso ahwehwɛ sɛ wɔyɛ mmara mu nsakrae na ama asiane a ɛwɔ nyinsɛn a wotu gu mu no ayɛ kɛse.
Awuraa Changamire se nhwehwɛmu pii kyerɛ sɛ mmeawa nkumaa nam nyinsɛn a wotu gu so rehwere wɔn nkwa.
Ɛwom sɛ mmabun pii rehwehwɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nsakrae wɔ mmara mu de, nanso mmea mpanyimfo bi sɔre tia, na wɔka sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ nyinsɛn a wotu gu ma ɛyɛ nea wogye tom kɛse, na wɔka sɛ ɛremma mmofra nni obu mma asetra.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie bi hyɛɛ Pregnancy Act nhyehyɛeɛ no ase afe 1977 mu ansa na ɔman no renya fahodie koraa.
Polisifo akyere MDC-T nnipa a Nelson Chamisa di wɔn anim no mu pii bere a wɔrebɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛhyɛn amanyɔkuo no adwumayɛbea ti a ɛwɔ Morgan Tsvangirai House no.
Yei bae berɛ a MDC kuo a Awuraa Thokozani Khupe di wɔn anim kyeree asoeɛ no.
Mfeɛ mmienu ni a Morgan Tsvangirai wuui no, Asɛnnibea Kɛseɛ abɔ Awuraa Khupe aba so sɛ ɔnkɔyɛ adwuma.
Polisifo a ɔda afiase no bi ne Chamisa asomfo baanu, Tendai Biti ne Lynett Karenyi Kore, ne David Chimhini, Lovemore Chinoputsa, Gladys Hlatywayo ne afoforo.
Wɔkaa sɛ nneduafoɔ yi nam kwan so rekɔ amanyɔkuo no adwumayɛbea ti, baabi a na polisifoɔ a wokurakura atuo atwa wɔn ho ahyia.
Studi7 ntumi ntee nnipa dodow a wɔakyere wɔn afi polisifo nkyɛn, na soboɔ a wɔabɔ wɔn sɛ polisi kasamafoɔ Paul Nyathi no nnyɛ ɔrekasa wɔ ne fon so.
Chamisa MDC kasamafo, fadzai Mahere kae sɛ kyere a wɔkyeree no no maa ne ho dwiriw no.
Tebea a ɛwɔ MDC no mu ayɛ den bere a Kɔɔto Baatan buu atɛn afe yi sɛ Chamisa ne Awuraa Khupe mmarahyɛbɛdwafie ahodoɔ no nnyɛ ɔmmarahyɛbɛdwafie na ɛwɔ sɛ wɔyɛ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie no berɛ a Awura Khupe na ɔhwɛ asafo no so.
Wɔ mmuaeɛ no akyi no, Awuraa Khupe yii mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu nnipa baanan ne mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu mmarahyɛbɛdwafie no mu nnipa nnyɛ wɔn amanyɔkuo no ananmusifoɔ bio.
Wɔn a wɔadi dɛm ne Thabitha Khumalo, Prosper Mutseyami, Lilian Timveous ne Charlton Hwende.
Zimbabwefo bi a wɔwɔ aman horow so ka sɛ wɔhyɛɛ wɔn sɛ womfi ɔman no mu esiane Robert Mugabe a wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔde abonnua na edi tumi no nniso nti.
Amammuisɛm ho nimdefo bi a ɔkyerɛ ade wɔ Bergen University a ɛwɔ Norway, ne Zimbabwe Yibuya / Mayibuye Zimbabwe ahyehyɛde no muni Dr Victor Chimhutu ka sɛ, ɛwom sɛ wobuu Owura Mugabe sɛ obi a ɔka Abibirem biakoyɛ ho de, nanso Zimbabwe abusua bi amfa no saa.
Dr. Chimhutu se, apam a Owura Mugabe ne Afrika akannifoɔ foforɔ bɔeɛ no yɛ adeɛ baako nti a wanya obu kɛseɛ afi Abibirem akannifoɔ hɔ.
Wɔka sɛ wɔbɛkae Owura Mugabe nso wɔ atɛnnidi ne atɛnnidi a ɔdaa no adi wɔ Atɔe fam aman te sɛ United States ne Britain mu.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ Owura Mugabe ammoro nkraman no ansie wɔn, sɛ ne Zanu PF amanyɔkuo no mufo sɔre tia wɔn, anaa mpo wɔyaw wɔn a wɔsɔre tia wɔn no a.
Wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ Owura Mugabe bɛhome Kwasida, ɛwom sɛ wonnya mmɔɔ ne tenabea ho amanneɛ de.
Nnuruyɛfoɔ ne ayarehwɛfoɔ a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ ayaresabea ahodoɔ aka akyerɛ aban sɛ, sɛ wontua wɔn ka ansa na December aba awieɛ a, wɔbɛgyae adwuma.
Ɔpanin a ɔda Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Nkabomkuo ano, Fortune Nyamande, a ɔkaa sɛ n’ahyehyɛde no ka Zimbabwe Ayarehwɛfoɔ Nkabomkuo no ho no kyerɛw krataa kɔmaa aban sɛ wɔnkɔ.
Dr. Nyamande kaa sɛ ɔkyerɛw aban sɛ ɔnka n’atuateɛ no nkyerɛ no afe a ɛdi hɔ, January 1 mu.
Wɔka sɛ wɔne ayarehwɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ Aban ayaresabea ahodoɔ atu saa anammɔntuo yi esiane sɛ ɛka a wɔbɔ wɔ akwantuo ho nni hɔ esiane sɛ wonnya nnyaa ɔsram biara akatua ne akatua a aban hyɛɛ ho bɔ nti.
Dr. Nyamande kasa tiaa ɔkwan a aban nam nsɛntwerɛfoɔ so kasa tia atesɛm nkrataa.
Sikasɛm Soafoɔ Patrick Chinamasa abɔ amanneɛ dada sɛ aban ntumi ntua n’adwumayɛfoɔ bi ka afe yi esiane sɛ wɔnni sika nti.
Dramande kaa sɛ, “Mr Chinamasa de atesɛm nkrataa abɔ nsakraeɛ a aba yɛn akatua berɛ mu no ho dawuru, enti yɛbɛfa akwan korɔ ara so.”
Wɔabɔ agumadi akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ a na wɔn nsa aka wɔn akatua Dwoada no dawuru Benada, nanso ɔmanfoɔ nyinaa, a dɔkotafoɔ ne ayarehwɛfoɔ ka ho, bɛnya wɔn akatua January 5 afe a ɛdi hɔ no.
Nanso aban asomfo pii a wɔne Studi 7 dii nkɔmmɔ no kae sɛ wonni ahotoso sɛ wɔn nsa bɛka wɔn sika wɔ mmere foforo no mu.
Yɛantumi ne Apɔmuden Soafoɔ, David Parirenyatwa, ne Apɔmuden Soafoɔ, Priscah Mupfumira ankɔhwɛ nea wɔbɛyɛ na atuateɛ no ankɔ so.
Ɔsɔretiafoɔ panin MDC amanyɔkuo no nwiinwii sɛ polisifoɔ reteetee emufoɔ.
Zimbabwe Mmaranimfoɔ a ɔhwɛ Hokwan a Nnipa wɔ so no se wɔakyere nnipa 47 nnansa yi, a wɔn mu fa kɛseɛ no ara yɛ MDC akyitaafoɔ ne asuafoɔ baason a wɔwɔ Allen Wilson Sukuu a ɛwɔ Harare sɛ wɔyɛɛ wɔn adeɛ wɔ mmara kwan so.
Nnipa a wɔakyere wɔn no bi ne Makomborero Haruzivishe a na ɔyɛ sukuuni panin a ofi ZINASU a ɔne ne yɔnko Allan Moyo kɔɔ kɔɔto nnɛ.
Yɛantumi ankasa antia Paul Nyathi a ɔyɛ Polisi kasamafo no esiane sɛ na wɔn tɛlɛfon nni ho mmuae nti.
Mmaranimfo Innocent Gonese, MDC mmaranimfoɔ, kaeɛ sɛ Haruzivishe ne Moyo bɛsan akɔ kɔɔto Dwoada abɛsusu asɛnnibea gyinaeɛ no ho.
Amanaman Nkabom Wiase Apɔmuden Ahyehyɛde (WHO) abɔ amanneɛ sɛ corona yare mmoawa a akunkum nnipa 233 wɔ China no abɛyɛ yareɛ a akɔ so wɔ wiase nyinaa.
Nnanu a atwa mu nkutoo no, wobu akontaa sɛ nnipa bɛyɛ 2,000 na anya corona yare no bi, na nnipa 9,800 na anya bi wɔ aman 244 mu wɔ wiase nyinaa.
WHO hene Dr. Tedros Adhanom Ghebreyesus kaa sɛ, berɛ a na wɔwɔ Chinafoɔ mu ahotoso sɛ ɔbɛyi yareɛ no afiri hɔ no, na wosuro sɛ sɛ ɛtrɛw kɔ wiase mmeaeɛ foforɔ a, ɛbɛtumi akum nnipa bebree.
Apɔmuden Soafoɔ Dr Obadiah Moyo se Zimbabwe rehwehwɛ nnipa bɛboro 200 a wofi China anaa aman foforɔ so a wɔanya corona yareɛ.
Wɔde nnipa a wɔwɔ nhwehwɛmu wɔ Zimbabwe no akɔ wɔn fie nnafua 14.
Apɔmuden soafoɔ a watwam Dr Henry Madzorera se Zimbabwe hia sika pii na ama yareɛ no atrɛ.
Ɔmanpanin a watwa mu Robert Mugabe funu bɛba Harare Wukuada awia na wɔde n’ayiyie no ho amanneɛbɔ bɛto dwa.
Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ nkitahodie so, Awuraa Monica Mutsvangwa bɔɔ eyi ho amanneɛ berɛ a ɔhyiaa ɔman no.
Awuraa Mutsvangwa kaa sɛ aban boayikuo ahodoɔ resiesie wɔn ho ama Owura Mugabe ayi.
Bere a wobisaa no nea enti a egyee bere tenten paa sɛ ɔbɛka Mugabe ayi ho asɛm no, Mutsvangwa ne Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ amamfrafoɔ nsɛm so Sibusiso Moyo kaa sɛ, “ɛyɛ nwonwa” sɛ ɔde n’ayi ho nhyehyɛeɛ bɛto dwa bere a Mugabe abusua a ɛwɔ Singapore no baa ɔman no mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ aban no ne Ɔmanpanin Mugabe abusua no reyɛ adwuma abom.
Ansa na saa bere no bɛba no, Ɔhene Katizagombo kasamafo, Gibson Jenami kae sɛ akasakasa biara nni Mugabe ayi no ho bio, efisɛ na aban a Emmerson Mnangagwa di wɔn anim wɔ saa dwumadie yi mu.
Ansa na saa bere no bɛba no, wɔde General General Trust Mugoba a ɔno nso wuui dapɛn a etwaam no bɛma no ahome Wukuada wɔ Acre amusie a ɛwɔ Harare no.
Wɔ amanneɛbɔ foforɔ mu no, Aban no se nsɛmmɔne a ɛrekɔ so wɔ South Africa no aka Zimbabwefoɔ 178 ma Zimbabwefoɔ mmienu na wɔawuwu wɔ saa nsɛmmɔne no mu.
Moyo kaa sɛ aban reyɛ nhyehyɛeɛ sɛ ɔde nnipa a wɔn ho aka no bɛba fie.
Aban no san kyerɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔyɛ apɔmuden adwuma, a dɔkotafoɔ ka ho, anya wɔn mfasoɔ ɔha mu nkyɛmu 60, na ɛnnɛ, aban no asi gyinaeɛ sɛ apɔmuden ne sika ho adwuma no bɛtena ase ahwɛ ahunu sɛ wɔbɛtua adwumayɛfoɔ no ka papa.
Apɔmuden Soafoɔ, Dr. Obadiah Moyo aka sɛ ɔbɛtena ɔman no sikasɛm asoeɛ nkyɛn ahwɛ ahunu sɛ aban mmarahyɛbɛdwafie yi bɛbam.
Nnawɔtwe a etwaam no dɔkotafo kɔɔ so teetee wɔn sɛ wɔn akatua sua dodo.
Ahyehyɛde bi a wɔtee sɛ wɔmfa nkae wɔn a wɔhwehwɛ nnipa kyɛfa ne kan Occupy Africa Unity Square kannifo Itai Dzamara a ɔyɛ Itai Dzamara Trust no di Amanaman Ntam Mmea Da.
Wɔyɛɛ dwumadie yi wɔ Highfield faako a wɔmaa mmea ne mmeawa a wɔkɔɔ dwumadie no nneɛma foforo, adwumayɛbea ne nea ɛkeka ho.
Dzamara abusua kasamafoɔ a ɔno nso yɛ Itai Dzamara Adwumakuo mu panin, Owura Partson Dzamara ka kyerɛɛ Studium 7 sɛ ɔhunuu sɛ ɛfata sɛ ɔda ɔdɔ adi kyerɛ mmea ɔsram yi, ɔsram a ne nuabarima Itai hweree no mfeɛ num a atwa mu no.
Ɔkaa sɛ ɛwom sɛ ne nuabarima no de ne ho ahyɛ amanyɔsɛm, hokwan a nnipa wɔ ne nsɛntwerɛfoɔ mu deɛ, nanso ɔyɛɛ ne nyinaa firii ɔdɔ mu na Itai Dzamara Ahotoso no bɛkɔ so ara ne no adi no ayamye so.
Ɔkaa sɛ n’ahyehyɛde no hyɛɛ n’adwuma ase wɔ Highfields akuraa ase efisɛ ɛhɔ ne bea a wɔwoo Itai nanso ɔkaa sɛ wɔbɛkɔ baabi foforɔ akɔboa mmea ne ahiafoɔ wɔ nimdeɛ ne osuahu wɔ nneɛma pii te sɛ mmara, nwomasua ne apɔmuden.
Wɔn a wɔde wɔn ho hyɛɛ nnwuma yi mu bi ne Rememberance Zuze a ɔkae sɛ ɛwom sɛ na wonnyaa Owura Dzamara de, nanso n’ani agye ahyehyɛde no nneyɛe a ɛhwɛ n’asetra so no ho.
Abeawa bi a wammɔ ne din ka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ wanya mfaso pii nnɛ.
Mprenpren no, Partson Dzamara abɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔbɛyɛ mfeɛ num nkaedie ama ne nuabarima a nnipa bi a wonnim wɔn kyeree no wɔ Glen View no Benada wɔ Harare.
Ɔkaa sɛ ɛde besi nnɛ no na wonnim baabi a ne nua no wɔ anaa sɛ́ ɔte ase no.
Ɔkae sɛ polisifo, wɔn a wɔpɛ nnipa kyɛfa, Zimbabwe Nnipa Kyɛfa Asoeɛ ne wɔn a wɔne Itai Dzamara yɛɛ adwuma no ka wɔn a wɔtoo nsa frɛɛ wɔn baa dwumadie no ase no ho.
Bere a wiase di aguanfo da, ɔkyena, no, Zimbabwefo bi a wɔte South Africa sɛ aguanfo no ka sɛ biribiara nni hɔ a ɛsɛ sɛ wodi ho ahurusi bere a South Africa wɔ ahokyere mu no.
Zimbabwefo bi ka sɛ South Africa nkyerɛ obu mma apam ahodoɔ te sɛ Amanaman Nkabom nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛfa aguanfoɔ ho no.
Ɔkyerɛwfoɔ panin a ɔda Zimbabwe Migrant Support Network ano, Shelton Chiyangwa, ka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ, ɛwom sɛ aguanfoɔ da no yɛ da a ɛho hia deɛ, nanso South Africa aguanfoɔ ho akyere wɔn.
Chiyangwa kaa sɛ Zimbabwe abusua a ɛte South Africa no nso ne nnipa atitiriw a wɔrehu amane.
Ɔkaa sɛ n’ahyehyɛde no ne Zimbabwefoɔ ne aman foforɔ reyɛ adwuma sɛdeɛ ɛbɛboa wɔn nsa aka akwantuo nkrataa.
Zimbabwe Exemption Permits a ɔyɛ panin abɛdiakyire, Gladys Mangwende kaa sɛ n’ahyehyɛde no ani gye aguanfoɔ adwuma no ho nanso nnipa kyɛfa a wɔnni ho asɛm na ɛhaw no.
Human Rights Watch a ɛwɔ Atifi Africa guamtrani, Dewa Mavhinga se aguanfo da no ho hia wɔ South Africa sɛnea Zimbabwefo pii te sɛ aguanfo no.
Owura Mavhinga kɔɔ so hyɛɛ South Africa aban no nkuran sɛ ɔmfa mmara no nyɛ adwuma, titiriw wɔ mmeae a atubrafo kɔ hɔ no.
Zimbabweni foforɔ a yɛfrɛ no George Manyika nso gyinaa Mavhinga asɛm no akyi.
Gabriel Shumba a ɔda Zimbabwe Exiles Forum ano asrɛ Amanaman Nkabom no, AU ne SADC sɛ wɔnhwehwɛ sɛnea SA ne aguanfo di nsɛm no mu yiye, titiriw Zimbabwefo.
Agyata no san srɛɛ South Africa soafoɔ, Aaron Motseledi sɛ ɔnnye ne dwumadibea mmara ntom sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɛrenhia sɛ aguanfoɔ pere ansa na wɔn nsa akɔ krataa so.
Ɔhyɛɛ nnipa bi nkuran sɛ wɔne n’ahyehyɛde no nyɛ adwuma na wɔnko mma aguanfoɔ nyinaa.
Aguanfoɔ no mu baako a yɛfrɛ no Francis Mukono kaa sɛ, na onhu sɛnea aguanfoɔ da no ho hia, efisɛ na tebea a ɛwɔ South Africa no yɛ den.
Oguanfo foforɔ a yɛfrɛ no Steven Chiweshe nso kaa sɛ onnim korɔnobɔ no.
Mandela Mad.) a ɔyɛ South Africa aguanfoɔ nsɛm ano kwankyerɛfoɔ panin no kaa sɛ n’adwumakuo no de krataa akɔ Amanaman Nkabom asoeɛ a ɛhwɛ nnipa Kyɛfa Asoeɛ so sɛ wɔmmoa wɔn mma wɔnsiesie ɔhaw a na wɔrehyia wɔ adwumakuo no mu no.
Maame kae sɛ ebedu ɔsram a edi hɔ no awiei no, n’adwumayɛbea no behu nea ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ de di saa nsɛm yi ho dwuma.
Wobu akontaa sɛ Zimbabwefo bɛboro ɔpepem abiɛsa aguan akɔ South Africa, abɔ aban soboɔ sɛ ɔde ateeteeɛ reba.
Nanso Zimbabwe aban se nnipa bi aguan akɔ nkuraase akɔpɛ adidibea papa.
Ayaresabea adwumayɛfo, a ayarehwɛfo ne dɔkotafo ka ho, ate atua bɛboro nnansa aka sɛ wɔn akatua nnɔɔso sɛ ɛbɛma wɔatumi akɔ adwuma a wonni anidaso biara sɛ wobenya ano aduru.
Tebea no mu ayɛ den wɔ aban ayaresabea ahorow, a wɔde ayarefo bi kɔ fie a wonnya ayaresa biara.
Yɛhwɛ kwan sɛ ayaresabea ahodoɔ no tebea bɛsɛe koraa berɛ a Senior Health Doctors Association de ato dwa dada sɛ, sɛ dɔkotafoɔ nketewa ne akɛseɛ no ansiesie wɔn sikasɛm ne wɔn amanehunu a, wɔn nso bɛkɔ so atua. Dɔkota a ɔda ayaresabea ahodoɔ no ano, Dr Aaron Musara ka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ nneɛma nkɔ yie wɔ ayaresabea ahodoɔ no mu.
Ɛwom sɛ na Dr Musara aka akyerɛ aban sɛ wabɔ ne tirim sɛ ɔbɛfa nkrataakyerɛw so akɔ nnwuma ahodoɔ no mu deɛ, nanso wɔannye ne ntom.
Ayarehwɛfoɔ a wɔwɔ ayaresabea ahodoɔ renyɛ adwuma na wɔrehyɛ aban sɛ ɔmfa US sika a wɔnyaa no October 2018 no mma wɔn akatua na ɔmma wɔn mfidie a wɔde bɛbɔ wɔn ho ban afiri yareɛ ho berɛ a wɔwɔ adwuma mu.
Ɔpanin a ɔda Zimbabwe Ayarehwɛfoɔ Nkabomkuo ano, ZINA, Enock Dongo se ɔkasa a ɔma wɔ aban anim no yɛ abirekyi ti.
Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Kuo (ZHDA) kasamafoɔ Dr Tapiwa Mungofa nso kaa sɛ apɔmuden adwuma a aban nni no ama ayarefoɔ nni ayaresa.
Owura Mungofa san kaa sɛ berɛ a mmofra no ayarehwɛfoɔ kɔɔ so teeteeɛ no, na wɔn mu pii wɔ fie sɛdeɛ wɔbɛbɔ wɔn ho ban wɔ COVID-19 ho.
Suapɔn a ɛtɔ so nson no antumi ante aban no afã wɔ ayaresabea adwumayɛfoɔ amanehunu no ho asɛm sɛdeɛ Ɔbenfo Amon Murwira a bere bi na ɔyɛ apɔmuden soafoɔ no antie ne frɛ wɔ telefon so no.
Nanso dapɛn a etwaam no, Owura Murwira bɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ ɔne ɔyarehwɛfo bi ahyɛ nkɔmmɔ ase. Ne mmofra abɛdiakyire John Mangwiro nso ka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ wonni adagyew sɛ wɔbɛkasa.
Apɔmuden Asoeɛ panin a ɔda Apɔmuden Asoeɛ ano, Dr. Paulinus Sikosana nso kaa sɛ wɔkɔɔ nhyiamu bi wɔ COVID-19 yareɛ no ho nti wɔantumi ne yɛn ankasa.
Apɔmuden ho abenfoɔ kyerɛ sɛ, sɛ aban anka ayarehwɛfoɔ a wɔbɛsan akɔ adwuma ho asɛm na wamma mmofra nnuruyɛfoɔ annyae gya, ɛnkanka seisei a COVID-19 yareɛ no akum nnipa 25 wɔ ɔman yi mu.

Nanso Owura Gotora kaa sɛ agyinatukuo no nsi adan a asɛe no nyinaa bio, na mmom wɔsi adan a kɔɔto no hyɛɛ nnipa nsia a wɔde agyinatukuo no kɔɔ kɔɔto no.

Owura Gwaru kaa sɛ n’awerɛhosɛm a ɛsen biara no mu baako ne sɛ, na ɔretua sika ama bagua no sɛ wɔnsi adwadie nhyehyɛeɛ papa. Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie pii a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu resɛe adan a wɔka sɛ wosii no mmara kwan so no.
Nanso aguadifoɔ a ɛwɔ wiase mmeaeɛ resɔre atia nea wɔn mmarahyɛbɛdwafie ahodoɔ reyɛ.
Bere a Kɔɔto Baatan buu atɛn Benada fa wɔn a ɛsɛ sɛ wodi MDC amanyɔkuo no anim firi bere a Morgan Tsvangirai wui no, nnipa pii pɛ sɛ wohu nea ɔyɛ Richard Morgan Tsvangirai House anaa Otwa Fie no wura ankasa ne no.
Kɔɔto no hyɛɛ Awuraa Thokozani Khupe sɛ ɔntwa MDC-T amammuo no nkosi sɛ wɔbɛtow aba wɔ asram abiɛsa mu.
Nanso ɔsɛmpɔw a ɛfa wɔn a wɔbɛhyɛn amanyɔkuo no adwumayɛbea ti hɔ no yɛ den kakra berɛ a nnipa mmienu na wɔrewɛn dan no, a wɔn din ne Ian Makone ne Reverend Tim Neil a na ɔyɛ Asɔre no panin wɔ Central Africa Mantam anaa CPCA mu.
Ɔkyerɛwfoɔ panin a ɔda MDC Apam ano, Charlton Hwende, gye di sɛ mfinimfini no hyɛ nnipa mmienu yi nsa, na wɔn nko ara na wɔma wɔn kwan sɛ wɔmfa nyɛ adwuma.
Douglas Mwonzora a ɔsan nso kyerɛ sɛ ɔyɛ amanyɔkuo no kyerɛwfoɔ panin asan aba amanyɔkuo no nkyɛn afe 2014 Ɔsan gye di sɛ amanyɔkuo no hyɛ Makone ne Neil nsa.
Nanso wɔkae sɛ wosusuw sɛ wɔbɛma wɔayɛ adwuma wɔ mo mu. Yɛantumi ne Owura Makone ne Owura Niel annya nkitahodie anka wɔn afã wɔ asɛm no ho.
MDC guamtenani abɛdiakyire a Nelson Chamisa, Hiob Sikhala di n’anim, se St Marys mpɔtam a ɛwɔ Chitungwiza no awo asebɔ a ɛreka amanyɛkuo akyitaafoɔ ma wɔaguan afi wɔn afie ahwehwɛ guankɔbea.
Sikhala a kan no na ɔyɛ Zengeza West MP no kae sɛ, na panin bi a ɔyɛ polisi adwuma a wɔfrɛ no Jabangwe a ɔwɔ mpɔtam hɔ rehwehwɛ n’akyitaafoɔ.
Yɛbɔɔ mmɔden sɛ yebehu Owura Jabangwe nanso na ɔmpɛ sɛ obua yɛn nsɛmmisa no.
Adesua a ɛtɔ so mmienu no nso yɛɛ den maa no sɛ ɔbɛte apolisi kasamafoɔ asɛm. Paul Nyathi a ɔyɛ Ɔsoafoɔ abɛdiakyire nti a ɔpɛ sɛ polisifoɔ kyere wɔn.
Nanso wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔsɛmpɔw a ɛfa kyere a wɔkyere MDC akyitaafoɔ ho no botaeɛ ne sɛ ɛbɛsɔre atia amanyɔkuo no atuateɛ a ɛrekɔ so wɔ ɔman no mu no.
Ɔsram a etwaam no, wɔkyeree Sikhala a wɔbɔɔ no sobo sɛ wabɔ pɔw sɛ ɔbɛsɛe Emmerson Mnangagwa aban no, ɔka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ nnipa pii reguan afi wɔn afie esiane sɛ wosuro sɛ wɔbɛkyere wɔn nti.
Nnipa bɛboro 90 na wɔkyeree wɔn wɔ Harare Fida a etwaam no wɔ atuatew bi a MDC yɛɛ ho nhyehyɛe saa da no ara mu.
MDC pɛ sɛ ɔtew atua wɔ nkurow akɛse a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu nanso polisifo de mmara ne banbɔ Apam no rebra amanyɔkuo no sɛ wɔnntoa wɔn atuateɛ no so.
Polisifo abara MDC sɛ wɔnnni atua wɔ Harare, Bulawayo, Gweru ne Masvingo.
Amanyɔsɛm mu nhwehwɛmufo se yei nso betumi asi wɔ Mutare faako a MDC bɔɔ ne tirim sɛ ɔbɛtew atua Yawda no.
Asɛnnibea Kɛseɛ atwe Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔyɛ Ɔtɛmmuafoɔ Ziyambi Ziyambi ne Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔyɛ Sikasɛm Soafoɔ Mthuli Ncube asensɛn sɛ wɔnntua MDC-T a Thokozani Khupe di anim no ho ka wɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie sikasɛm ho mmara ase.
Asɛnnibea Kɛseɛ Temmufoɔ Priscilla Munangati Manongwa de too dwa Yawda sɛ ɔntwe Ziyambi ne Ncube aso sɛ wɔmfa MDC-T amanyɔkuo a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛyɛ amanyɔkuo a ɛhyɛ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie ase no mma amanyɔkuo no.
Ɛrenkyɛ na MDC no nsa aka R7,500 wɔ RTGS mu.

Nanso Morgen Komichi a ɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔyɛ amanyɔkuo no guamtenani wɔ Asɛnnibea Kɛseɛ atɛmmuo a ɛse Chamisa antie ne amanyɔkuo mmara sɛ ɔbɛyɛ MDC kannifoɔ no kaa sɛ ɔbɛfa akwan bi so anya sika no sɛdeɛ ɔyɛ amanyɔkuo no kannifoɔ.
Nanso Owura Tamborinyoka kae sɛ ɔwɔ sika no ho kwan bere a MDC MP no de ne din hyɛɛ mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu no.
Nanso Komichi kaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ Owura Chamisa ne afoforo di mmara so.
Mprenpren mu no, Harare mmaranimfoɔ, Kudzai Kadzere kaa sɛ wɔde nnafua du pɛ na bɛtumi de asɛm no akɔdan kɔɔto no.
Ziyambi de telefon so ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ, sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔkasa tia atɛmmuo no sɛdeɛ kɔɔto no hyɛeɛ a, wɔn nso wɔde wɔn nkrataa no bɛkɔ kɔɔto wɔ nnafua du ntam.
Yɛantumi ne Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie Kasamafoɔ, Jacob Mudenda, anaa Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ sikasɛm so no annya nkitahodie annya n'afã wɔ asɛm yi ho sɛdeɛ ɔno nso din wɔ kɔɔto nkrataa mu no.
Mmaranimfoɔ bi se kɔɔto no de ahyɛdeɛ too dwa sɛ, sɛ wɔannye Chamisa MDC asɛm no antom a, Kɔɔto no bɛtumi ayɛ n’adwene sɛ ɔde sika no bɛkɔ Chamisa MDC.
Ɛnyɛ eyi ne bere a edi kan a MDC ako afa saa sika yi.
Wɔ afe 2006 mu no, berɛ a MDC kyerɛwfoɔ panin Welshman Ncube sɔre tiaa Morgan Tsvangirai wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako akyi no, ɔkɔɔ so nyaa MDC sika no nyinaa maa amanyɔkuo no, na ɛmaa Owura Tsvangirai a ɔyɛ amanyɔkuo a ɔdɔɔso wɔ mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu no nni kaprɛ baako pɛ.

Abasobɔ no kyerɛ sɛ mmea a wɔwɔ wiase afanan nyinaa wɔ akokoduru, na United States Department of International Relations na ɛde ma.
Dr. Nyampinga kae sɛ onsusuw da sɛ obenya nidi a ɛte saa, na ɔkae sɛ ɛyɛ no anigye sɛ wɔahu ɔne mmea foforo 11 a wofi wiase afanan nyinaa.
Dr. Nyampinga se wɔbɛtu kwan akɔ United States mmeae ahorow asua afiase tebea ahorow ho ade sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi ahyɛ wɔn fie adwuma mu den.
Dr. Nyampinga se wɔn adwuma no gye akokoduru, na ɛyɛ wɔn anigye sɛ afoforo ahu adwuma a wɔreyɛ wɔ fie no.
Ɔrekasa wɔ dwumadie no ase no, Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ Amanaman Ntam Nkitahodie so Michael Pompeo kaa sɛ adwuma a mmea 12 yi reyɛ no yɛ anigyeɛ na ɛgye akokoduru.
Mfe 14 ni a yefii dwumadie no ase.
Mmea a wɔanya abasobɔdeɛ yi bi ne Afghanistan, Armenia, Azerbaijan, Bolivia, Burkino Faso, Kazakhstan, Malaysia, Nicaragua, Pakistan, Syria, Yemen ne Zimbabwe.
Owura Pompey kaaɛ sɛ saa dwumadie yi ho hia paa berɛ a ɛmaa mmea nyaa kwan yɛɛ adwuma maa afoforɔ a wɔwɔ wiase afanan nyinaa.
Ɔrekasa wɔ dwumadie no ase no, ɔbaa a odi kan a ofi United States, Melania Trump, kaa sɛ n’ani agye adwuma a mmea reyɛ wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa no ho.
Ɔkae sɛ efi bere a edi kan a wohyiaa mmea a wɔapaw wɔn sɛ wɔnnye wɔn ntom mfe anan a atwam ni no, wɔakɔ so ahyia mmea a wɔreyɛ adwuma pa wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa ɛwom sɛ wɔn mu bi yɛ saa nnwuma yi na wɔteetee wɔn nanso wɔkɔ so yɛ saa.
Dr. Nyampinga se ɔhyɛɛ n'adwuma ase sɛ obi a ɔhwehwɛ nnipa kyɛfa wɔ amanyɔsɛm mu mfeɛ aduasa ni.
Wɔ ne amanyɔkuo akyi no, Awuraa Nyampinga yɛ Zimbabwe Mmaa Nkabom Kuo, Crisis in Zimbabwe Coalition, Women Academy on Political Leadership Excellence ne Women And Aids Support Network no panin.
Zimbabwefo mmea a wɔanya abasobɔdeɛ no bi ne Awuraa Jenni Willaims, Awuraa Magodonga Mahlangu, Awuraa Jestina Mukoko ne Awuraa Beatrice Mtetwa.

Nhwehwɛmu bi a China yɛe wɔ Zimbabwe kyerɛ sɛ ɛnte saa. South Africa National Institute of Communicable Diseases wɔ animdefoɔ a wɔwɔ South Africa atifi fam paa sɛ wɔbɛhwɛ sɛ ebia obi anya coronavirus anaa.

Ban a wɔbaraa fagudeɛtubea ne bɔs ahodoɔ a ɛhyɛ ZUPCO bɔs adwuma ase no de ɔhaw ahodoɔ aba, na ama nnipa a wɔahyiamu wɔ bɔs gyinabea ahodoɔ berɛ a ɔman no rebɔ mmɔden sɛ ɛbɛtrɛw Covid-19 yareɛ no mu wɔ ɔman no mu.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ nnipa pii rehu amane esiane sɛ wonni lɔre ka nti, titiriw anwummere a ɛma wɔde wɔn ho hyɛ bɔs kakra a ɛwɔ hɔ no mu.
Aban ahyɛ mmara sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ hyɛntiafoɔ fa nnipa wɔ COVID-19 yareɛ no berɛ so sɛ ɔkwan a ɔbɛfa so asiw yareɛ no ano, berɛ a ɔkyerɛɛ mu sɛ bɔs a ɛwɔ ZUPCO nko ara na ɛsɛ sɛ ɛfa hyɛntiafoɔ.
Nanso bɔs ne bɔs ahodoɔ bi wɔ hɔ a, wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔmpɛ sɛ wɔbɛhyɛ saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi ase, a nneɛma bi te sɛ akwannya a ZUPCO de tua sika no ka ho.
Dwoada no, wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔyɛ bɔs ho adwuma no ne ZUPCO mpaninfoɔ hyiaa mu sɛ wɔnni wɔn haw ahorow ho dwuma, a wɔn bɔs ahorow ka ho.
Benada no, na wɔhwɛ kwan sɛ bɔs ahorow no ne aban mpanyimfo behyia na wɔasiesie akasakasa no.

Nanso ɔpanin a ɔda Harare Residents Trust ano, Precious Shumba, kaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ aban di akwantuo ho nsɛnnennen no ho dwuma ntɛm pa ara ansa na nneɛma akɔ soro.
Agyata kyerɛ sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ aban de polisifo, asraafoɔ anaa asafo mu polisifoɔ si bɔs gyinabea hɔ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛhwɛ ama mmara ayɛ adwuma na abɔ nnipa ho ban na yareɛ no antrɛw.
Wɔsan ka sɛ, ɛsɛ sɛ apɔmuden adwumayɛfoɔ nso kyinkyin bɔs gyinabea ahodoɔ hwɛ sɛ wɔyɛ nnipa a wɔmpɛ HIV anaa Covid-19 ho asɛm.
Nnwuma a ɛwɔ Bulawayo ne nkuropɔn ahyehyɛde ahorow ahyia kuropɔn mu mpanyimfo ne wɔn asusuw ɔhaw a wɔkyerɛ sɛ nsu ho yɛ na, a wɔkyerɛ sɛ egyee bere tenten no ho.
Adwadie Fekuw a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe (ABUZ) panin Victor Nyoni kaa sɛ saa dwumadie yi asɛe nnwuma bebree adwuma esiane sɛ wɔn akwaa no hia nsu na wɔde ayɛ wɔn da biara da dwumadie nti.
Owura Nyoni kaa sɛ mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu mpaninfoɔ a ɔhyiaa wɔn no ahyɛ no bɔ sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ nsuo kwan dapɛn a ɛdi hɔ no mfiase, berɛ a mmarahyɛbɛdwafie no hwɛɛ kwan sɛ ɛbɛwie n'adwuma wɔ dapɛn no awieɛ.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ Bulawayo kuropɔn ahyɛn nnawɔtwe a ɛtɔ so mmienu no mu a nsu nni mu bere a agyinatukuo no yɛɛ nsakraeɛ sɛ wɔbɛsiesie mfidie a wɔde yɛ nsuo wɔ Criterion Nsuo Adwuma no.
Wɔsan ka sɛ yei yɛ nsu a ɛresɛe wɔ baabi a nsuo wɔ wɔ Criterion ne Magwegwe, ɛna anyinam ahoɔden dwumadie a wɔde popa nsuo mu.
Owura Nyoni se nnipa pii nim sɛ Bulawayo kuropɔn no adi boro mfeɛ 120, na mfidie ne nsuo ho durubɛn nso adi mfeɛ dedaw.

Odwumayɛni a ɔhwɛ adwuma no so, Dr. Prince Butau kaa sɛ ɔrehwɛ kwan sɛ obetie Owura Mlogagwa asɛm Yawda anaa Fida biara.

Zimbabwefo bi a wɔwɔ South Africa atew atua wɔ Groote Schuur Ayaresabea a ɛwɔ Cape Town, faako a Ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire Constantino Chiwenga rehwɛ no, rehyɛ no sɛ ɔnsan nkɔ ayaresabea bi a ɛwɔ ɛhɔ.
Wɔbɔ amanneɛ sɛ woyii Owura Chiwenga fii ɔman no mu dapɛn awiei kɔɔ ayaresabea wɔ South Africa, ɛwom sɛ Studi 7 antumi anhu adanse biara a ɛkyerɛ sɛ na ɔwɔ ayaresabea a ɛsõ sen biara wɔ South Africa.
Nsɛm Ho Amanneɛbɔ Soafoɔ Monica Mutsvangwa ne Information Secretary Nick Mangwana ampene so sɛ ɔbɛka asɛm no Kwasida berɛ a fononoo a ɛtɔ so nson a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe no ne no dii nkitaho no, ɔhyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnkyere George Charamba.
Nanso Studium 7 antumi anhyia Charamba ansa sɛ ɛyɛ nokware sɛ na Chiwenga yare na wɔrehwɛ no wɔ ayaresabea anaa.
Zimbabweni foforɔ a yɛfrɛ no Carlos Chimbi a ɔte Cape Town bɛkaa Zimbabwefoɔ ho wɔ atuateɛ no mu.
Chimbi kaa sɛ “ɛyɛɛ no awerɛhow paa” sɛ ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire abɛbu nnipa a wɔadi dɛm a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu animtia, efisɛ na onim sɛ sɛ ɔyare a ɔbɛhwehwɛ ayaresa wɔ amannɔne.
Ɔkae sɛ n’ani agye sɛ otumi kaa n’asɛm kyerɛɛ ayaresabea no sɛ ayaresabea panyin aka akyerɛ no sɛ ɔne no nkasa, ɛwom sɛ wanka sɛ Owura Chiwenga wɔ ayaresabea hɔ anaa onni hɔ de.
Chimbi kaa sɛ ayaresabea panin aka akyerɛ no sɛ mmara mma no kwan sɛ ɔnka ayarefoɔ a wɔwɔ ayaresabea hɔ a wɔnni ayaresabea hɔ no ho asɛm.
Afe a etwaam no, Chiwenga hyɛɛ nkurɔfo no abufuw bere a dɔkotafo kɔɔ so teetee wɔn sɛ wɔnyɛ adwumayɛfo a wɔn ho akokwaw na mmom wɔyɛ adwumayɛfo a wɔba fam, ne sɛ aban no nnyɛɛ nhyehyɛe a ɔde bedi ɔhaw ahorow a ɛwɔ ayaresabea ahorow a ɛma nkurɔfo hwere ayaresa a ɛmfata no ho dwuma.
Groote Schurr Ayaresabea no agye din yiye sɛ wiase no mu nea edi kan a wɔde koma kɔ koma foforo mu.
Polisi abara ɔsɔretiafoɔ panin MDC amanyɔkuo no sɛ ɔnni nsawɔsoɔ ɔkyena berɛ a wɔhwɛɛ kwan sɛ amanyɔkuo no kannifoɔ, Nelson Chamisa bɛbɔ amanyɔkuo no akwankyerɛ ne ne nhyehyɛeɛ ho dawuru afe yi no.
Ɔrekasa wɔ amanyɔkuo no Standing Committee nhyiamu a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Harare no akyi no, MDC kasamafo abɛdiakyire, Luke tamborinyoka kaa sɛ polisifo abara saa dwumadie yi na ɔkae sɛ wɔn ani abere resan abue sukuu ahorow.
tamborinyoka kaa sɛ wɔrenyɛ nhyiamu yi ɔkyena efisɛ na MDC pɛ sɛ n’akyitaafoɔ kwati sɛ polisifoɔ bɛhwe wɔn anaa wɔbɛtow ahyɛ wɔn so.
Ɔkaa no pefee sɛ na polisifoɔ no rebɔ mmɔden sɛ wɔbɛtow ahyɛ amanyɔkuo no akyitaafoɔ so sɛdeɛ wɔyɛeɛ berɛ a amanyɔkuo no yɛɛ wɔn adwene sɛ wɔbɛte atua wɔ nkuro ne nkuraase a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu nyinaa ara no.
Ɔkae sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nhyiamu a wɔfrɛ no Agenda 2020 no wɔ Awuraa Musodi Hall a ɛwɔ Mbare Benada a edi hɔ no wɔ baabi a wɔde bɛto dwa akyiri yi.
Owura tamborinyoka kaa sɛ MDC no abrɛ esiane sɛ wobu no sɛ amumuyɛfoɔ ahyehyɛdeɛ na ɔresusuw ho sɛ ɔbɛkɔ so adi mmara so anaa ɔbɛsesa ne nhyehyɛeɛ nti.
Yɛante sɛ Zimbabwe Republic Polisi, ZRP kasamafo, Paul Nyathi, a ɔyɛ ɔsoafo abɛdiakyire no reka sɛ wɔn telefon a wokura kyin no nyɛ adwuma nti.
Amanyɔsɛm mu nhwehwɛmufo a wɔfrɛ no Masimba Kuchera a ɔno nko ara yɛ adwuma no ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ ɔtee nka sɛ polisifo rehaw MDC no.
Afe a etwaam wɔ Oforisuo mu no, ZRP bɔɔ MDC ho ban sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ɔyɛkyerɛ wɔ nkuropɔn ne nkuraase a atwa ɔman no ho ahyia mu, efisɛ na wosuro sɛ atuateɛ no bɛkɔ akowie basabasayɛ mu sɛnea esii wɔ January mu no.
Wɔabɔ Etiopia man soafoɔ Abiy Ahmed din sɛ ɔmfa afe yi Nobel Peace akyɛdeɛ no mma. Norway de saa abasobɔdeɛ yi ma.
Ahmed kamfoo no sɛ ɔde asomdwoe baa ɔman no ne Eritrea ntam wɔ mfe 20 ɔko a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ aman mmienu no ntam.
Obibini a odi kan a onyaa abasobɔde no ne Albert Luthuli a ofi South Africa wɔ 1960 mu.
Wɔn a wɔnyaa bi nso ne Nelson Mandela a wawu a ofi South Africa, Anwar Sedat a ofi Misraim ne Kofi Annan a ofi Ghana.
Nnipa foforɔ a wɔdii nkunim no bi ne Ɔsɔfopɔn Desmond Tutu a ɔtenaa ase wɔ Liberia Ɔmanpanin Ellen Johnson Sirleaf ne Wangari Maathai a ɔfiri Kenya a ɔno ne abibini bea a ɔdi kan wɔ Abibirem.
Wɔ afe 2011 mu wɔ Zimbabwe no, wɔpaw Ɔmanpanin a watwa mu Ɔsoafoɔ Morgan Tsvangirai sɛ ɔmma no akyɛdeɛ ɛwom sɛ wantumi anni nkonim deɛ.
Dr. Pedzisayi Ruhanya a ɔyɛ amanyɔsɛm ho nimdefo wɔ University of Johannesburg se Ɔmanpanin Emmerson Mnangagwa wɔ nneɛma pii sua fi Ahmed akwankyerɛ mu.
Ɔkɔm ne nsu rekum asono ne mmoa foforo bebree wɔ Hwange National Park, na ɛrekanyan aban no ma wayere ne ho sɛ ɔbɛte asono dodow so.
Wɔ Studi7 nsrahwɛ a ɛwɔ Hwange National Park mpɔtam no, yehuu asono pii a aduan pa a wonnya nni ama wɔawuwu wɔ mmeae bi afe yi.
Zimbabwe Parks and Wildlife Management Authority kasamafo (Zim Parks) Tinashe Farawo ka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ asono 85 na wɔawuwu fi September mu, na bɛboro 200 na wɔawuwu afe yi esiane ɔkɔm nti.
Nea ɛka kɔm no ho bio ne sɛ, nneɛma a ɛma nnipa wuwu no mu baako ne aduane ne nsu a ɛho ayɛ na, na ama asono ne mmoa foforo dodoɔ so ate.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ sɛ ɔsono bi didi a, ohia aduan a emu duru boro kilogram 500, na nsu a emu duru boro galɔn abien.
Nanso mprempren Simparks bu akontaa sɛ asono bɛboro 45,000 na wɔwɔ mpɔtam hɔ.
Nnipa bi a wɔhwehwɛ mmoa kyɛfa ka sɛ nkonta a Simparks de ama no yɛ atoro, na wɔka sɛ wɔreyɛ eyi sɛ ɔkwan a wɔnam so hwehwɛ mmoa na wɔatumi atɔn asono.
Nnipa a wɔtwe wɔn aso wɔ asase so, a wɔfrɛ no Lenin Chisaira, gye tom sɛ ɔkɔm de asono ne mmoa foforo na wonnya aduan pa nni, nanso ɔka wɔn a wɔtaa Simparks akyi no ho.
Sɛdeɛ Chisaira kyerɛ no, adeɛ baako a ɛma ɔkɔm de mmoa wɔ Hwange National Park no ne gyinaeɛ a aban asi sɛ ɔbɛma nnipa kwan ma wɔayɛ nneɛma bi te sɛ faga tu a wɔka sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ wɔ hɔ.
Nanso Owura Farawo kaa sɛ n’adwenem yɛ no nãã wɔ adwene a wɔn a wɔrehwehwɛ mmoa ho kwan no wɔ wɔn adwenkyerɛ ho. Wɔkae sɛ wɔmpɛ sɛ wogye tom sɛ, esiane adwuma pa a n’adwumakuo no reyɛ nti, asono ne mmoa foforo renya nkɔanim. Ɔde kaa ho sɛ, dwumadie no ho da hɔ na wɔn a wɔpɛ sɛ wɔhu nea ɛrekɔ so wɔ mmoa yɛmmea hɔ nyinaa bɛtumi akɔ hɔ.
Zimbabwe ne Afrika atifi fam aman foforo, a Botswana ka ho, se wɔpɛ sɛ Amanaman Ntam Adwadie Ho Nhyiamu a ɛwɔ Endagered no ma wɔn kwan sɛ wɔbɛtɔn wɔn asono sɛdeɛ mmoa dodoɔ anya nkɔanimɛ a ɛde ɔhaw pii aba, a nnipa ne mmoa a wɔbɔ wɔn tuo ka ho.
Afe yi nkutoo no, ahyehyɛde no mu mmoa akunkum nnipa aduasa mmiɛnsa.
WƆ CITES nhyiamu bi ase wɔ Geneva, Switzerland wɔ Oforisuo mu no, ahyehyɛde no bɔɔ nsa a wɔde too wɔn anim sɛ wɔnnyi asono ne wɔn asonse ho anohyeto no gui.
Kwankyerɛfoɔ a ɔda Safari Operators Association a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe ano, Emmanuel Fundira, kaa sɛ ɛhia sɛ CITES ne wɔn a wɔhwehwɛ mmoa ho kwan no bɛte ɔhaw a Zimbabwe ne aman foforɔ refa mu no ase, esiane asono dodoɔ a wɔwɔ saa aman yi mu nti.
Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ wim tebea ne nsrahwɛ so, Nqobizitha Ndlovu, ka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ aban no rebɔ mmɔden biara sɛ ɔne aman foforɔ bɛyɛ adwuma ama CITES anya ntease foforɔ.
Nanso wɔsan ka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ wobetumi atu akɔ aman foforo so akɔtɔn asono wɔ aman foforo a ɛwɔ CITES a wɔatu anammɔn koro no ara mu.
Wobuee Hwange National Park wɔ afe 1928 mu na ɛno ne ɔman no mu mmoa yɛmmea a ɛso sen biara.
Ahyehyɛde no kɛse boro akwansin 14,000, na wobu akontaa sɛ asono bɛyɛ 2,000 pɛ na wɔwɔ.
Ɔkyerɛwfoɔ Panin a ɔda Zimbabwe bɔɔlbɔkuo ano, FUZ, Paul Gundani wuui Wukuada awia bere a na yareɛ bi abɔ no.
Nanso yennim ɔkwan a nneɛma kɔɔ so.
Sɛdeɛ FUZ kyerɛ no, Gundani wuui wɔ Topomasi Private Hospital a ɛwɔ Kwekwe.
Bɔɔlbɔkuo no san se wɔn akwantuo no ama akwansini kɛseɛ a ɛbɛyɛ den sɛ wɔbɛtoto mu, berɛ a wɔn ani abere sɛ wɔbɛboa bɔɔlbɔkuo no.
Gundani a bere bi a atwam no ɔbɔɔ bɔɔl maa Zisco steel no nso bɔɔ bɔɔl maa Mmofra Akofoɔ no berɛ a na wɔfrɛ bɔɔlbɔkuo no "Dream Boayikuo" wɔ Reinard Fabisch a watwa mu no akwankyerɛ ase.
FUZ nsɛntwerɛfoɔ panin Marlene Gadzirayi kaa sɛ ne ho dwirii no sɛ ɔtee sɛ Gundani awu.
"Mema me werɛ how yiye sɛ me ne wɔn kasaa ɛnora na yɛreyɛ nhyehyɛe sɛ yɛbɛtoa so. Nanso ɛnnɛ mete sɛ wɔayera nanso saa bere yi de, minnim nea Owura Gundani dii," Awuraa Gadzirayi ka kyerɛɛ Studio7.
Awuraa Gadzirayi se ɔman no ahwere bɔɔlbɔ mu dɔmmarima kɛseɛ bi. Awuraa Gadzirayi nso se na ɔnni nhyehyɛe biara sɛ ɔbɛyɛ Owura Gundani ayi berɛ a na ɔretwɛn sɛ n’abusuafoɔ bɛgye n’ahome no.
Zimbabwe Football Association (ZIFA) de ato dwa wɔ wɛbsaet hɔ sɛ Gundani wu no ama ne werɛ ahow na n’abusuafoɔ bɛsɔre agyina n'ayie nhyehyɛeɛ nyinaa mu.
ZFA nkitahodie dwumayɛni Xolisani Gwesele kaa sɛ Gundani wu no yɛ ɔman no awerɛhosɛm, na ɛbɛyɛ den sɛ wubenya ɔbarima bi a n’ani gye bɔɔlbɔ ho.
Gwesela kyerɛwee wɔ ZIFA wɛbsaet no so sɛ, “W’asomdwoeɛ nka Paul Gundani.”
Ɔmanpanin a watwa mu Robert Mugabe funu antumi ankɔ ne fie wɔ Zvimba nnɛ berɛ a ne yere Grace Mugabe yareɛ.
Abusuafo bi ka sɛ nipadua no bedu Zvimba Dwoda.
Nnipa bɛyɛ apem atwɛn Ɔmanpanin Mugabe funu dakoro wɔ Zvimba awia yi.
Ɔkasamafo ma Mugabe abusua no, a ɔno nso yɛ nea wawu no banana, Leo Mugabe kaa sɛ, nteaseɛ bi nti na ɔkae sɛ ɔnnim sɛnea Ɔhene Zvimba somaa no.
Leo Mugabe kaa sɛ nipadua no bɛba fie anɔpa.
Nanso Ɔhene Katizagombo a wɔsan frɛ no Gibson Jenami kaa sɛ nipadua no nsan nkɔ Zvimba sɛnea na wɔhwɛɛ kwan fi bere a Awuraa Grace Mugabe yareeɛ no.
Ɔhene Katizagombo nso kaa sɛ nipadua no bɛhyɛ aban nsa kɔpem da a ɔde bɛma no ahome.
Nanso eyi ne Leo Mugabe a ɔkae sɛ n’abusua bɛkora Mugabe funu so kosi sɛ wobewie abantenten damoa no bɔ abira.
Adwenem naayɛ a ɛrekɔ so wɔ Ɔmanpanin Mugabe ayi ase no ama nnipa pii ho adwiriw wɔn sɛ ebia Mugabe funu no bɛba sɛnea na ɛte bɛyɛ nnafua 30 ansa na wɔasie no no.
Leo Mugabe kaa sɛ, Mugabe funu no bɛdi da koro wɔ Zvimba na asan akɔ Harare akɔgye n’ahome.
Leo Mugabe kaa sɛ nnipa ahyia faako wɔ Ɔmanpanin Mugabe fie wɔ Harare.
Ɔsɔretiafoɔ MDC-T a Nelson Chamisa dii n'anim a ɔno nso hwɛɛ kwan sɛ ɔbɛwu wɔ Zvimba nnɛ, Lloyd Tarubwa a ɔfiri Banket a wɔkyeree no too afiase asram akron a wɔanni n’asɛm no, kaa sɛ wɔbaa abɛhwɛɛ sɛ Ɔmanpanin Mugabe awu ampa anaa.
Sɛnea wɔyɛɛ Owura Mugabe ayi no ama nnipa pii ho adwiriw wɔn wɔ ɔman no mu a wɔkyerɛ sɛ Owura Mugabe amanehunu a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ ne mmerɛberɛ mu no na ɛkɔfaa ne wuo baeɛ.
Owura Mugabe wui wɔ Singapore wɔ September 6 bere a na ɔyare mfe pii no.
Amalgamated rural Akyerɛkyerɛfoɔ Kuo a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe, anaa ARTUZ se, wɔn kannifoɔ no mu baako a ɔne Godfrey Chanda na ɔkyeree no de no too afiase nnɔnhwerew mmienu wɔ Gweru a na ɔmanfoɔ nnim ho hwee.
Nanso wɔagyae Chanda a ɔyɛ ArtUZ boayikuo a ɛwɔ Midlands mantam mu no, bere a wɔhyɛɛ no sɛ ɔne agumadi akyerɛfoɔ nhyiamu wɔ Gweru no.
ARTUZ Ɔmanpanin Obert Masaraure kaa sɛ woyii Chanda adi bere a bɔɔlbɔkuo a ɔwɔ ne nnanu atuateɛ no mu kɔɔ so yɛɛ nnansa atuateɛ no.
Masaraure se adwadie fekuw bi nso reko sɛ ɛbɛboa wɔn nkabom.
Ɔyɛkyerɛ no ba awiei Wukuada.
Masaraure kaa sɛ wɔbɛyɛ nhyiamu bi wɔ atuateɛ no akyi sɛ wɔbɛyɛ ho nhyehyɛeɛ.
Yɛantumi ne Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔhwɛ Adwumayɛ so, Awuraa Sekai Nzenza ankɔhwehwɛ aban gyinabea wɔ asɛm no ho nanso wɔnnyaa ne mobile fon ho mmuaeɛ.
F.F. Plato agyinaeɛ mpofirim wɔ Caf Champions League no ama nsɛmmisa pii asɔre wɔ Zimbabwe bɔɔlbɔ ho.
Ɛwom sɛ wɔda so ara agyaw agodie mmienu wɔ akansi no mu deɛ, nanso FC Platinum rentumi nnyina Esperance a ɔwɔ agodie awotwe no ano, na saa ara nso na wɔrentumi mmoro Horoya Athletic Club a ɔwɔ agodie ason no wɔ fie ne abɔnten a Horoya na ɔhwee wɔn wɔ mu a ɛno ne nea edi kan a sɛ saa akuw yi wie agodie no pɛpɛɛpɛ a, wɔhwɛ.
Mprempren, FC Platinum wɔ agodie anan mu bɔɔl biako pɛ, enti wɔredi agoru a aka no awie sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobenya obu ama Spencer Mushambadope fɛ a ɔka ho no.
Mushambadope se abasobɔ biara remfi akansi a aka no mu mma.
Afe a etwaam no, Angola manpanin de August yii saa kuw koro no ara adi bere a Lunda bɔɔ wɔn wɔ fie bio no.
Wɔ afe 2017 mu no, Caps United duu akansi no fã ketewa no nanso wɔantumi ankɔ n’awiei bere a Al Ahli Tripoli a ɛwɔ Libya hwee no 4-2 wɔ fie no.
Saa afe koro no ara mu no, Angolani Libolo bɔɔ Ngezi Platinum Stars a na wogyina Zimbabwe ananmu wɔ Caf Confederation mu no tuo fii agodie no mu.
Wɔ afe 2016 mu no, wɔbɔɔ Harare City a na ɔno nso wɔ saa akansi koro no ara mu wɔ Zambia Zanaco amanneɛbɔ a edi kan mu bere a wɔhwee no 2 - 2 wɔ Rufaro Agumadibea na wowiee 3 - 1 wɔ Zambia.
Yei kyerɛ sɛ ɛhɔnom akuw no nnyɛ wɔn ade te sɛ Abibirem akuw foforo no te sɛ nea na ɛte mfeɛ a atwam no, bere a Dynamos sii akan wɔ ɔkwan a etu mpɔn so sɛ ɔbɛduru Caf Champions League a ɛtwa to wɔ 1998 mu ne nea ɛtwa to wɔ afe 2008 mu no.
Nea ɛyɛ yaw kɛse ne sɛ FC Platinum wɔ agodie anan mu pɛnkoro, wɔnnhwehwɛɛ asɛm biako mu, ne bio nso, wɔde nsia ama wɔ agodie anan mu.
Asɛmmisa no ne sɛ, sɛ bɔɔlbɔkuo bi rebɔ bɔɔlbɔkuo ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe nyinaa ara na wɔredi saa bɔɔlbɔkuo yi wɔ Afrika a, ɛkyerɛ sɛn?
United kyɛfafoɔ Tinashe Musebi se bɔɔlbɔ agyigya araa ma ɛho abɛhia sɛ wɔyɛ nsakraeɛ bebree ansa na Zimbabwe akuw ahodoɔ a ɛbɛn Lesotho, Botswana ne Swaziland bɔɔ fam.
Bɔɔlbɔ ho nkyerɛkyerɛmufo Farai Kambamura se Zimbabwe akuw no nnyɛ wɔn ade wɔ Afrika efisɛ bɔɔlbɔkuo a ɛboaa wɔn ma wɔbɔɔ wɔn din wɔ Zimbabwe no rekɔ amannɔne, titiriw South Africa berɛ a wɔresi akan wɔ Afrika no.
Afe a etwaam no, FC Platinum hweree Gerald Takwara, Elvis Chipezeze ne Talent Chawapiwa, afe yi mu Rodwell Chinyafanere a odii nkunim wɔ bɔɔlbɔ mu nkonim wɔ afe nkonimdi mu a ɔkɔɔ Baroka no.
Nanso John Chiko a odii Lengthens bɔɔlbɔkuo no anim wɔ Premier Soccer League mu no kaa sɛ ɛwɔ sɛ Zimbabwe bɔɔlbɔkuo no bɛdɔɔso wɔ ɔman no mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a bɔɔlbɔkuo ahodoɔ no betumi atua bɔɔlbɔkuo no ka sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔrennwane nkɔ South Africa ne Zambia.
Seisei, Zimbabwe wɔ bɔɔlbɔkuo mmienu pɛ, Castle Lager Premier Soccer League ne Chibuku Super cup. Wɔbɔɔ Zifa cup no wɔ afe 2005 mu.
Obi a n’ani gye bɔɔlbɔ ho, Musa Masepe, ka sɛ Zimbabwe nni bɔɔlbɔ ho nimdeɛ biara esiane sɛ bɔɔlbɔfo pɛ sɛ wɔto nnwom anaa biribi foforo esiane sɛ wɔn akatua wɔ bɔɔlbɔ mu yɛ den nti.
Sɛ eyi kɔ so a, ebegye bere ansa na mo hɔnom akuw ne Afrika akuw foforo asi akan.
Abatoɔ a wɔde bɛgyina Democratic Party ananmu wɔ US mmarahyɛbɛdwafie abatoɔ mu no rekɔ so wɔ abatoɔ a ɛda kan New York sohwɛfoɔ Michael Bloomberg ano.
Bloomberg a wabɛyɛ ɔdefo paa no amfa mmirikatɛntɛ annyina ne amanyɔkuo ananmu wɔ ɔmampanyin abatoɔ a ɔne Republican Amanyɔkuo kasamafoɔ, Donald Trump bɛsi akan no mu.
Owura Bloomberg bɔɔ amanneɛ wɔ November afe a etwaam no mu sɛ ɔde ne ho rehyɛ amanyɔkuo no mu, na ɔsɛee sika bɛboro dɔla ɔpepem 400 wɔ aguade ho dawurubɔ mu. Saa sika yi yɛ wɔn dea.
Ɔdefo yi amfa ne ho anhyɛ abatoɔ a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Iowa ne New Hampshire no mu, na saa ara nso na ɔremfa ne ho nhyɛ abatoɔ a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Navada ne South Carolina no mu ansa na abatoɔ a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Ɔbɛnem abatoɔ mu no adu, berɛ a amantam 14 bɛpaw obi a ɔbɛgyina Democratic Party ananmu wɔ US aban abatoɔ mu.
Bere a Bloomerg de ne nan sii fam peree dwumadie no, amanyɔkuo no mu nnipa bi te sɛ Bernie Sanders a ɔyɛ Vermont ananmusini wɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu ne Elizabeth Warren a ɔyɛ Massachusetts ananmusini wɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu no fii ase sɛee Bloomberg din no.
Ɔrekasa wɔ Nevada amanyɔkuo anim no, Owura Sanders kaa sɛ, nea ɛbɛyɛ na ne amanyɔkuo no adi Owura Trump so nkonim no, na ohia obi a obetumi aboaboa nnipa pii ano sen bere biara wɔ Amerika abakɔsɛm mu.
Owura Sanders kaa sɛ Owura Bloomberg yɛ obi a nnipa bebree nim no yiye wɔ gyinaeɛ a New York kurow sohwɛfoɔ sii sɛ ɔbɛsɛn abibifoɔ na wahwehwɛ wɔn a wɔyɛ abibifoɔ ne wɔn a wɔn bra asɛeɛ no. Ɔkaa sɛ, saa akwantuo no ntumi mma nnipa pii mma wɔnto aba mma Owura Trump yi fi hɔ wɔ November mu.
Nanso Bloomerg kasa tiaa Owura Sanders nsɛm, bere a ɔkae sɛ Owura Sanders a ɔredi nhyiamu ahorow anim no abɛyɛ Democratic Party abɔdin wɔ ɔmampanyin abatoɔ a ɛbɛhyɛ Owura Trump nsa mfeɛ nan a ɛdi hɔ no.
Amanyɔsɛm mu nhwehwɛmufo bi ne Zanu PF panin, Frank Guni, kaa no pefee sɛ akansi no fa Sanders ne Bloomberg ntam, ɛwom sɛ na ɛda adi pefee sɛ seesei Sanders wɔ akyitaafoɔ bebree deɛ.
Guni se, wɔ ne nsusuwii mu no, ɛsɛ sɛ Sanders ne Bloomberg bom tu mmirika wɔ abatoɔ abatoɔ no mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛdi Trump so nkonim.
Nnipa bi a wɔabɔ wɔn din wɔ Democratic Party mu ka sɛ; Barack Obama, a watwa mu, Joe Biden; Minnesota mmarahyɛbɛdwani Amy Klobuchar, ne kan South Bend kurow sohwɛfo a ɔwɔ Indiana, ne ɔbarima a ɔwɔ bɔbeasu koro a ɔne no wɔ bɔbeasu koro, Pete Buttigieg.
Democratic Party wɔ ananmusifoɔ 3,979, na sɛ wɔbɛpaw obi ama abatoɔ abatoɔ no a, ɛsɛ sɛ ɔnya ananmusifoɔ 1,990.
Ananmusifoɔ yi akyi no, ananmusifoɔ a wɔkyɛn so nso wɔ hɔ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a sɛ wɔyɛ Democratic Convention no wɔ Ayɛwohomumɔ wɔ Wisconsin a, ananmusifoɔ ne ahwɛsofoɔ 4,750 na ɛwɔ hɔ, na wɔn a wɔbɛto wɔn wɔ saa nhyiamu yi ase no bɛnya nnipa 2,200. Nnipa aduoson asia na wɔbɛto aba.
Nnipa pii kɔ sikakorabea ahorow anɔpa sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobenya sika de ahyɛ wiase sikakorabea kɛseɛ no bɔ nanso wɔatumi ayi afunibufuo a aporɔw afi hɔ.
Nhwehwɛmu bi a Studi 7 yɛe wɔ Sikakorabea ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ Harare, Bulawayo, Chinhoyi, Masvingo, Mutare, Gweru ne nkuropɔn foforɔ mu daa no adi sɛ Sikakorabea biara nnyaa sika foforɔ yi, na sikakorabea bebree ntumi mmaa nkurɔfoɔ dedaw no.
Jossam Marwira a ɔka sikakorabea adwumayɛfoɔ ho no kaa sɛ ɔretwɛn sika no da koro berɛ a ɔtee sɛ wɔde sika foforɔ bɛka ho no.
Owura Marwira kaa sɛ, nea ɛhaw no paa ne sɛ ɔbɛtɔ sika wɔ abɔnten, na ɔkae sɛ, ɛbɛyɛ papa sɛ nnipa a wɔte sɛ ɔno bɛnya sika afi sikakorabea ahodoɔ hɔ kwa.
Ɔbarima bi a ɔtɔ sika na ɔtɔn wɔ kwan ho a wammɔ ne din no nso ka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ ɔrehwɛ sika foforo no kwan nanso wanhu hwee.
RBZ, Sikakorabea Kɛseɛ no de too dwa nnansa yi sɛ ɔde nnwuma foforɔ bɛhyɛ ɔman no sikasɛm mu ahokyereɛ mu.
RBZ Amammuo John Mangudya de ato dwa sɛ ɔde sika kɔkɔɔ sika dɔla mmienu ne dɔla mmienu bɛto hɔ sɛnea ɔhwɛɛ kwan sɛ ɛbɛyɛ adwuma nnɛ.

Zimbabwefo a wɔka kar wɔ South Africa no ho adwiriw wɔn wɔ kar ahorow a South Africafo a wosusuw sɛ wɔmpɛ sɛ amamfrafo hwehwɛ adwuma hyew no ho.
South Africa aban asoafoɔ a ɔyɛ polisifoɔ, Bheki Cele; Akwantuo Soafoɔ fikile Mbalula; ne Ɔsoafoɔ a ɔyɛ Adwumayɛfoɔ, Thulas Nxesi ne afirikafoɔ a wɔreka lɔre, wɔn a wɔrehwehwɛ adwuma ayɛ ne wuranom yɛɛ nhyiamu bɔɔ wɔn kɔkɔ sɛ wɔnyɛ wɔn a wɔrehye lɔre no.
Na lɔre akɛse a wɔrebɔ wɔn kɔkɔ no wɔ gya mu sɛ wɔbɛkyere wɔn sɛ wɔresɛe sikasɛm.

Nsɛnkyerɛwfo nso Shumba akasa atia wɔn sɛ wɔanka asɛm no ankyerɛ ɔmanfoɔ.
Agyata kɔɔ so kae sɛ wɔn ahyehyɛde no akyerɛw nkrataa akɔ amamfrafoɔ nnwuma a ɛwɔ South Africa, a Zimbabwe ka ho, sɛ wɔmmom nyɛ adwuma mfa mpopa ɔhaw no.

Fida no Zimbabwe bɛkaa wiase nkae nyinaa ho wɔ Amanaman Ntam Mmea Da no ase, a mmea pii ka sɛ wɔda so ara hyɛ wɔn so na wɔbɔ wɔn ka efisɛ ɔman no mu akannifo mpɛ sɛ wɔbɛhyɛ wɔn nkuran ama wɔanya akwannya koro.
Ɛwom sɛ Zimbabwe wɔ mmara bi a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ mmea ne mmarima nyinaa yɛ pɛ de, nanso mmea a yɛkaa wɔn ho asɛm sɛ ɛho nhia sɛ aban mpaninfoɔ, amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ, asɔre ahodoɔ anaa nnwuma hwɛ ma saa asɛm yi si.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie ne mmaranimfoɔ panin a watwa mu, Awuraa Jessy Majome, ka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ, mmarima a wɔyɛ wɔn adwuma sɛ akannifoɔ na wɔn amanehunu yɛ kɛseɛ wɔ ɔman yi mu.
Wɔka sɛ hokwan kɛse wɔ hɔ sɛ ɔman no bɛtoto mmea ne mmarima ntam, sɛ wodi mmara so a.
Zimbabwe Mmea Mmaranimfoɔ Kuo panin, Abigail Matsvai, ka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ ɛnnɛ yɛ da a ɛho hia paa, na wɔde rehyɛ aban mpaninfoɔ nkuran sɛ wɔmfa mmara a ɛma mmarima ne mmea nyinaa hokwan yɛ pɛ nni dwuma.
Awuraa Tsungirai Hungwe-Chimbunde a ɔka wɔn a wɔhwɛ ɔbarima ne ɔbea nna so ho no ka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ nhomasua a ɛyɛ den ho hia na ama ɔmanfo ahu hia a hokwan ahorow a ɛwɔ mmaa ne mmarima ntam no ho hia.
Ɔkaa sɛ n’adwuma no reyɛ nea obetumi biara sɛ ɔbɛkɔ amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ nkyɛn ama wɔn manfoɔ hokwan pɛ wɔ abatoɔ no mu sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a mmea pii bɛtu mmirika akɔyɛ adwuma.
Afe yi afahyɛ ahorow no asɛmti ne, Think Equal, Build Smart, innovative for Change.
Awuraa Majome kaa sɛ, nea ɛne asɛmti yi hyia no, abatoɔ adwumakuo no mfa saa tumi yi mma mmaa ne mmarima nkongua pɛ wɔ abatoɔ 2023 mu.
Awuraa Matsvai aboa saa ɔsesɛw akuw yi wɔ akanni mu.
Awuraa Majome nso kaa sɛ ɛho hia sɛ mmea bɛka wɔn ho abɔ mu na wɔako atia wɔn ntɔkwaw, na ɛnyɛ sɛ mmarima bɛsisi wɔn.
Ɔkaa no pefee sɛ mmarima pii a wɔwɔ adwumayɛbea no mpɛ sɛ wofi amanyɔkuo no mu, ɛno nti na na wɔne mmea reko na ɛmma wɔn kwan mma wɔnkɔ adwuma no.
Wɔhyɛ Amanaman Ntam Mmea Da no ho fa afe biara wɔ Ɔbɛnem 8 sɛ ɛyɛ ɔkwan a wɔfa so hyɛ mmea mpuntuo ho nkuran wɔ sikasɛm, amanyɔsɛm ne nneɛma foforo mu, na wɔboa ma mmea ne mmarima nyinaa yɛ pɛ wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa.
Aban mmarahyɛbɛdwafie kɔɔ so wɔ Gokwe a ɛwɔ Midlands mantam mu, na ahyehyɛde pii nso kɔɔ so wɔ mmeae ahorow. Ná MDC kannifo Nelson Chamisa rehyɛ saa da no agyirae wɔ Chitungwiza.
Nsɛm ho amanneɛbɔ adwumayɛbea foforo a ɛwɔ hɔ nnɛ, a Zimbabwe Asoeɛ a Ɛhwɛ Nnipa Kyɛfa So ka ho, kaa sɛ ɛyɛ den ma mmea sɛ wɔbɛkɔ wɔn anim wɔ mprempren sikasɛm tebea mu esiane sɛ obiara amma wɔn kwan nti.
Zimbabwe Peace Project asan de ato dwa sɛ ɛda a wɔbɛtew atua atia hokwan a nnipa wɔ sɛ wɔde di dwuma ɔkwammɔne so, a nea ɛka ho ne nnipa kyɛfa a wɔde di dwuma ɔkwammɔne so wɔ Ɔbɛnem bosome mu wɔ ɔman no mu.
Adwumayɛfoɔ Kɔɔto no asi gyinaeɛ sɛ, sɛ mmofra nni adwumam a, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔsan kɔ adwuma nnɔnhwere nnwɔtwe mu, efisɛ wɔn dwumadie no mmara mma ho kwan.
Adwumayɛ Asɛnnibea temmufo Rodgers Manyangadze ne Lawrence Murasi ama dɔkotafo no nnanu sɛ wɔnsan nkɔ adwuma.
Asɛnnibea no sii gyinae nso sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde akasakasa a ɛda mmofra no dɔkota ne aban ntam no kɔdan ntamgyinafo ansa na wɔadi asɛm no ho dwuma wɔ nnafua 14 mu.
Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Kuo panin abɛdiakyire, Dr. Masimba Ndoro kaa sɛ atɛmmuo yi nyinaa akyi no dɔkotafoɔ mfata sɛ ɔkɔ adwuma.
Studi7 bisabisaa wɔn sɛ ebia wosuro sɛ wɔn nnwuma befi wɔn nsa sɛ wɔanni kɔɔto ahyɛdeɛ so a, Dr. Ndoro ka kyerɛɛ adwumawuranom sɛ wɔnyɛ biribi mfa mpagya adwumayɛfoɔ mma wɔnkɔ adwuma.
Mmaranimfoɔ a ɔda Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Fekuw ano, Doug Coltart kaa sɛ ɔne no nyɛ adwene, na mmom ɔbɛhwehwɛ nea enti a ɔyɛɛ saa no mu.
Ɔsan nso kaa sɛ ɔwɔ hokwan sɛ ɔde asɛm no kɔto Kɔɔto no anim wɔ atɛmmuo no ho, sɛ dɔkotafoɔ pɛ sɛ wɔyɛ ho biribi a.
Studi7 antumi antie apɔmuden soafoɔ, Dr. Obadiah Moyo ne Apɔmuden Asoeɛ,
Dɔkotafoɔ no kɔɔ so te atua September da a ɛtɔ so mmiɛnsa no. Wɔkae sɛ wonni adwuma yɛ.
Dɔkotafoɔ mpanyimfoɔ a wɔaka wɔ adwumam nso tenaa ase nnawɔtwe a etwaam no de nwiinwii faa akatua ne ayaresabea ahodoɔ ho.
US aban se Cyclone Idai sɛee Manicaland mansini no na saa awerɛhosɛm yi bɛkɔ so aha manfoɔ.
Berɛ a ɔne Studi 7 rekasa wɔ US ananmusini, Jason Taylor, USAID kwankyerɛfoɔ a ɔhwɛ atoyerɛnkyɛm ho dwuma so no, ɔkaa sɛ berɛ a na wɔne nnwumakuo foforɔ reyɛ adwuma de asiesie akwan na wɔresisi adan a asɛe no, seesei wɔde wɔn adwene asi aduane a ɛbɛbɔ wɔn nkwa ho ban no so kɛse.
Taylor kaa sɛ ɔhaw a ɛrekɔ so wɔ Manicaland no mu yɛ den araa ma Zimbabwe aban no ankasa ntumi nyɛ ho hwee.
Taylor a ɔde Wiase Aduan Dwumadie no helikopta kɔɔ Manicaland mansini mu no kaa sɛ ɛyɛɛ no ahodwiriw sɛ ohuu adwenemhaw wɔ ɔmantam no mu.
Ɔkae sɛ mmofra a ohuu wɔn no nni anigye. Ɔkae sɛ ɛho hia sɛ bere a Manicalandfo anya nneɛma te sɛ aduan ne dan mu mfaso no, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔboa wɔn ma wɔn ho san wɔn.
Taylor san kaa sɛ, wɔ Chimanimani ne Chipinge no, wɔanhu wɔn a wɔtete hɔ a wɔkyerɛ sɛ amanyɔkuo a wɔtaa akyi no mmoa wɔn no, na saa ara nso na wɔanhyia wɔn.
USAID asan aka sɛ wɔwɔ nimdeɛ a wɔde bɛtete Zimbabwefoɔ ma wɔahwehwɛ wim tebea mu ahu bere ne beae a ahum no bɛba, ne nea wɔbɛtumi ayɛ de asiw nkwa ne agyapadeɛ sɛ aban ka sɛ wɔnsɛe no ano.
Efi bere a Cyclone Idai pae gui no, United States ama Zimbabwe sika dɔla ɔpepem 2.6.
Ansa na saa bere no bɛba no, aban, Amanaman Nkabom ne ahyehyɛde ahorow a ɛnyɛ aban de sika dɔla ɔpepem aduosia ama Cyclone Idai.
Wobu akontaa sɛ nnipa bɛyɛ 300,000 hia mmoa wɔ Manicaland mansini mu, na wɔn mu 129,000 yɛ mmofra nkumaa.
Wɔ mansini akron a Cyclone Idai sɛee no mu no, wɔsɛee sukuu ahorow 113, na ɛmaa asuafo 90,000 hweree wɔn afie.
Aban se nnipa bɛboro 300 na wɔnni ho akontaa, na nnipa foforo 399 na wowuwui wɔ akwanhyia no mu.
Yɛhwɛ kwan sɛ saa nnipa yi bɛdɔɔso.
Ayarefo bi ka sɛ wɔrehwɛ wɔn wɔ amannɔne bere a mmofra ayarehwɛfo a wɔka sɛ wosuro sɛ ebia wobewuwu wɔ ayaresabea ahorow a wonni ayaresa biara ateetee wɔn no.
Nhwehwɛmu bi a Studi 7 yɛe ada no adi sɛ ayarefo bi atu kwan seesei akɔ aman foforo te sɛ South Africa, Botswana ne Zambia so akɔhwɛ mmofra no wɔ ɔyarehwɛfo ntua no akyi.
Ayarefo a yɛne wɔn kasae wɔ Parirenyatwa no mu baako a wɔfrɛ no Awuraa Molline Chindove kaa sɛ ɔbaa ayaresabea hɔ nna kakra sɛ ɔrebɛsa yareɛ nanso na biribiara nkɔ yie.
Awuraa Chindove kaa sɛ ɔrekɔ South Africa akɔhwɛ sɛ osuro sɛ sukɔm bekum no wɔ nsu no mu.
N’abusuafo no mu baako a wɔfrɛ no Fiona Muchabaiwa kae sɛ ɔnni biribiara yɛ sɛ ɔde ne yarefo no bɛkɔ Zambia ɔkyena akɔhwɛ no, na ɔkae sɛ ne boɔ yɛ den dodo.
Nhwehwɛmu bi a Studi 7 yɛe ada no adi sɛ aban ayaresabea ahodoɔ a wɔato mu no ama nnipa pii regyae ayaresabea ahodoɔ a wɔhwɛ wɔn wɔ ankorɛankorɛ ayaresabea ahodoɔ.
Wilbert Kasanze kaa sɛ ɔgyee ne yere firii Chegutu ayaresabea kɔɔ ankorɛankorɛ ayaresabea bi a ɛwɔ Chitungwiza.
Kasanze se da biara da bɔs kwan a ɔfa fi Chegutu baabi a ɔte kɔ Chitungwiza no rema ne sika a ɔde ahyɛ ne kotoku mu no agyae.
Apɔmuden Asoeɛ abɔ amanneɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔhwɛ mmofra a wɔakɔ pɛnhyen no bɛsan akɔ adwuma ntɛm ara.
Afei nso adwumakuo no hyɛɛ wɔn a wɔrepɛ adwuma no nyinaa sɛ wɔnnyae adwuma no, na wɔhyɛɛ wɔn nkuran sɛ sɛ wɔn da so ara pɛ adwuma a, wɔnsan mfa wɔn adwuma mmɛyɛ.
Yei di asɛm bi a Ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire Constantino Chiwenga de too dwa sɛ ayarehwɛfoɔ a wɔn ho yɛ hu nyinaa nnyae adwuma no.

Messi kaa saa nsɛm yi berɛ a copa America agodie no kɔɔ so wɔ United States, berɛ a Argentina hweree n'adeɛ a ɛtɔ so mmienu wɔ Chile berɛ a Chile maa nkontabuo no soɔ no.

Bere a wiase no hyɛ October sɛ Breast Cancer Awareness Month no, Cancer Association a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe no se ɛhaw nnipa bi a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu sɛ wɔnte wɔn ase.
Ahyehyɛde no bɔ amanneɛ sɛ nnipa pii a wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔanya kokoram no, nea edi kan no, wɔkɔ dɔkota a ɔhwɛ adwene ne nneyɛe so, na afei wɔkɔ dɔkota a ɔwɔ yare a emu yɛ den ho nimdeɛ nkyɛn, na ɛma ɛyɛ den sɛ wɔbɛsa.
Cancer Association of Zimbabwe fotufo Priscilla Mangwiro kaaɛ sɛ, sɛ obi wɔ ɔhaw no a, ɛhia sɛ ɔkɔ dɔkota a ne ho akokwaw nkyɛn.
Awuraa Mangwiro se ɛho hia sɛ wɔhwehwɛ nnipa a wɔanya kokoram no mu, titiriw nufu mu kokoram.
Awuraa Mangwiro se nufu mu kokoram ne ade a ɛtɔ so mmienu a ɛma mmea wuwu wɔ Zimbabwe.
Awuraa Mangwiro se efi October 1 a ɔhyɛɛ n'atu ase sɛ ɔbɛhyɛ October sɛ Cancer Awareness Month no, n’ahyehyɛde no asɔ mmea bɛboro 50 ahwɛ, na wɔn dodow bɛkɔ so akɔ soro akosi ɔsram yi awiei.
Berɛ a ɔtee Cancer Association of Zimbabwe dwumadie no ho asɛm no, ɔbaa bi a wɔfrɛ no Gertrude Magwaniza kaa sɛ ɔde ne babea no hyɛɛ ne nufu mu.
Awuraa Mangwiro se nneɛma pii na ɛma mmea tumi nya nufu mu kokoram.
Awuraa Mangwiro se ɛsɛ sɛ wɔhwɛ mmea wɔ wɔn nufu mu nsakrae ahorow ho, na sɛ wɔyɛ saa a, ɛsɛ sɛ wɔhwehwɛ wɔn mu ntɛm ara.
Awuraa Mangwiro se nnipa pii susuw sɛ, sɛ wohu sɛ wanya kokoram a, ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔrewu nanso nneɛma pii wɔ hɔ a wobetumi ayɛ de aboa ama mmea anyin akyɛ.
Awuraa Mangwiro se nneɛma a ɛde kokoram ba no mu biako ne sɛ obedi aduan a srade ne asikre pii wom.
Awuraa Mangwiro rehyɛ mmea nkuran sɛ wɔmfa hokwan a wɔanya wɔ October mu no nyɛ nhwehwɛmu wɔ kokoram ho, na wɔnkyerɛkyerɛ wɔn yareɛ no ho.

Ɔrekasa wɔ mmarahyɛbɛdwafie wɔ fango boɔ ho no, Godfrey Ncube a na ɔyɛ ɔpanyin wɔ Petrotrade so no kaa sɛ, sɛ nnwumakuo nya kwan sɛ wɔbɛtɔ fango na wɔatɔn no wɔn ankasa sika mu nkutoo a, ɛnna ɔbɛtumi ayɛ saa.
Owura Ncube gye toom sɛ saa a ɔbɛyɛ no bɛma ne bo akɔ soro nanso ɔkae sɛ ɛno ne ɔkwan koro pɛ a ɔnam so beyi fango ho haw a ɛda ɔman no ano bere tenten no afi hɔ.
Owura Ncube kaa sɛ, bere a aban no retwɛn sɛ ɔde fango bɛma wɔn no rebrɛ fango bo ase wɔ ɔman no mu, berɛ a na wɔregye fango pii no.

Awuraa Magombo kaa sɛ ɔbea no ntumi nkyerɛ bere a saa nhyehyɛeɛ yi bɛkɔ yie, ɛwom sɛ Owura Mangudya ka kyerɛɛ boayikuo no ɔsram a etwaam no sɛ ɔwɔ anidasoɔ sɛ wɔde krataa no bɛyɛ adwuma sɛdeɛ wɔpɛ sɛ wɔyɛ no.

Owura Chirisa kaa sɛ ayarefoɔ a wɔwɔ aban ayaresabea ahodoɔ no yareɛ no yɛɛ kɛseɛ berɛ a dɔkotafoɔ nkumaa ne dɔkotafoɔ 533 na wɔgyee wɔn too hɔ berɛ a Apɔmuden Asoeɛ no tuu kwan no.

Chiwenga a ɔhyɛ aban ase sɛ ɔnni nkabom a ɛda aban ne dɔkotafoɔ a wɔn ho yɛ hu no ntam no, bɔɔ ayarehwɛfoɔ paa wɔ atuateɛ no akyi.
Nnipa pii a wɔkyerɛ sɛ Owura Chiwenga de asraafoɔ redi dwuma wɔ nsɛm a ɛhia nkitahodie ho akasa atia wɔn nneyɛɛ.
Mmerante ne mmabaa a wɔyɛ dɔkotafo ka sɛ wɔpɛ sɛ aban ma wɔn nnwinnade a wɔde sa yare, nnuru ne ntade a wɔde bɔ wɔn ho ban, bere a wɔwɔ adwuma mu, ne akatua a wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɛte sɛ ɔkraman tow.
Nanso aban se ne ntoboa no so ate araa ma ɛyɛ den sɛ ɔbɛma akɔ soro.
Yɛante apɔmuden soafoɔ Owura Obadiah Moyo asɛm yie berɛ a ɔne oduruyɛfoɔ a ɔhwɛ mmofra yareɛ yɛɛ nhyiamu berɛ a yɛdii kan kɔɔ wim no.
Aban Asɛnnibea no abɔ aban abisade no agu, efisɛ aban mfaa nkrataa biara mmaa wɔn wɔ wɔn asɛm a ɛfa dɔkotafoɔ a wɔrenyɛ adwuma no ho.
Doug Coltart a ɔyɛ mmaranimfoɔ a ɔgyina Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Kuo ananmu wɔ Labor Court no kaa sɛ kyerɛwtohɔ a ɛfiri Apɔmuden Adwumayɛfoɔ Panin,HSB hɔ nnɔɔso nti yɛrentumi nni asɛm no wɔ mmara kwan so.
Kɔɔto no hyɛɛHSB mmaranimfo no sɛ ɔmfa nkrataa a ayera no mma ɔkyena, Wukuada.
Nanso dɔkotafoɔ aka sɛ, ɛnyɛ kɔ a wɔbɛkɔ kɔɔto no ne adeɛ a ɛbɛma wɔakɔ adwuma, enti ɛnni ɔhaw no ho dwuma.
Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Kuo panin abɛdiakyire, Dr. Masimba Ndoro kaa sɛ n’adwuma no hwehwɛ sɛ ɔyɛ biribiara a ɛsɛ sɛ ɔyɛ da biara da.
Nnuruyɛfoɔ nketewa yi kɔɔ so teɛteɛɛ wɔn ho wɔ September da a ɛtɔ so mmiɛnsa no mu sɛ wɔnni sika a wɔde bɛyɛ adwuma.
Nnuruyɛfoɔ a wɔn mfe akɔ anim a wɔfiri Zimbabwe Senior Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Nkabomkuo mu nso kɔɔ so teetee Yawda a atwa mu yi, berɛ a na wɔreka sɛ wɔn akatua sua na wonni aduruyɛ mu sika.
Dɔkotafoɔ a wɔn mfe akɔ anim no nso kyerɛw krataa de bɔɔ wɔn kɔkɔ sɛ, sɛ dɔkotafoɔ no kɔ ayaresabea a, ɛbɛyɛ den sɛ wɔbɛgye wɔn nkwa.
Nnuruyɛfoɔ no kasa tiaa aban no nso, na wɔka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔn sika no akɔ soro ɔha mu 60, na wɔka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔn adwene nhyia wɔ ho.
Mprenpren mu no, Zimbabwe Sukuupɔn no atua nnuruyɛfoɔ mpanyimfoɔ mmienu bi ka wɔ soboɔ a wɔbɔɔ wɔn sɛ wɔde wɔn ho rehyɛ atuateɛ no mu na wɔhyɛɛ afoforɔ ma wogyaee nom no ho.
Dr. Bothwell Mbuvayesango a ne ho akokwaw wɔ mmofra oprehyɛnyɛ mu ne Dr. David Chimuka a ɔyɛ komayare ho nimdefo.
Dr. Mbuvayesangano gyee din wɔ ɔman no mu berɛ a wɔyɛɛ no ntaafoɔ oprehyɛn wɔ afe 2014 mu na Dr. Wake nso yɛɛ no oprehyɛn wɔ komayare mu.
Zimbabwe Association of Doctors for Human Rights akasa atia denneennen sɛ Dr. Mbuvayesangano ne Dr. Get sɔre.
Yɛnte firi Zimbabwe Sukuupɔn hɔ, na saa ara nso na yɛnte firi aban hɔ wɔ apɔwmuden ho nsɛm ho.
Nanso asɛm bi a Apɔmuden Soafoɔ Obadiah Moyo kaeɛ kyerɛɛ sɛ dɔkotafoɔ anni aban asɛm a ɔde too dwa sɛ ɔnsan nkɔ adwuma no so.
Moyo kaa sɛ aban no retwɛn asɛm no awieɛ, na ɔkyerɛɛ sɛnea tebea no teɛ.
Dɔkotafoɔ kɔɔ so teɛteɛɛ wɔn so September 3, na wɔka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ wonni sika a wɔde bɛkɔ adwuma.
Aban no ne adwumakuo bi a ɛwɔ amannɔne ayɛ apam sɛ wɔbɛboa ma wɔde gyabiriw akɔ aman bi te sɛ India ne Japan mu.
Bere a ɔne Victoria Consulting rekasa wɔ apam no nkrataa ase no, fagudeɛtubea Soafoɔ, Winston Chitant kaa sɛ aban botaeɛ ne sɛ ɔman no benya kwan atɔ gyabiriw wɔ India na wahyehyɛ sika ama fagudeɛtubea adwuma.
Chitando kaa sɛ wobu akontaa sɛ fango tɔn ɔpepem aduonu num na ɛwɔ Zimbabwe nanso fango tɔn ɔpepem mmienu kɔpem mmiɛnsa na wotu fango afe biara.
Chitando san kaa sɛ India ne ɔman a ɛsõ sen biara a wɔtɔn gyabiriw afe biara, sɛ wɔde toto aman foforo ho a.
Bere a ɔrekasa wɔ nhyiamu koro no ara ase no, ɔmanpanin Emmerson Mnangagwa kaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ Zimbabwe de abusuabɔ pa a ɛda ɛne India ntam no di dwuma.
Studi7 ntumi nkyerɛ Victoria Consulting adwumakuw ko a ɔne wɔn ayɛ adwuma, ne wɔn mpanyimfo.
Nanso ɔsoafoɔ abɛdiakyire a ɔda fagudeɛ mu ahonyadeɛ ano, Gift Chimanikire, kaa sɛ ɔnhunu hia a ɛho hia sɛ Zimbabwe hwehwɛ nnwuma a ɛbɛma wɔatumi akɔ amannɔne akɔtɔn fango a seesei fango nnɔɔso wɔ ɔman no mu.
Sikasɛm ho nimdefoɔ bi a wɔfrɛ no Nyasha Muchichwa nso kaa sɛ, wanhu hia a ɛho hia sɛ Zimbabwe hwehwɛ adwumakuo bi a ɛyɛ amamfrafoɔ a wɔn ani gye Zimbabwe nnyinasoɔ ho.
Owura Muchichwa kaa sɛ ɛyɛ papa sɛ ɔne aman foforɔ bɛdi nsawɔsoɔ.
Ministry of Minerals wɛbsaet no se Zimbabwe wɔ gyabiriw a eye sen biara, na ɛwɔ mmeae 29 a wotu gyabiriw.
Nnwuma mmienu pɛ na ɛwɔ ɔman yi mu, Hwange Colliery ne Mountain Resources, na wɔyɛ galamsey adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔsõ sen biara.
Wɔagyae MDC-T amanyɔkuo no mu nnipa baasia a Nelson Chamisa di wɔn anim a wɔkyeree wɔn wɔ Harare Fida no mu biara wɔ $ 1,000 fi wɔn afie mu.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwani Chancellor Bianca Makwande, Chamisa asoafoɔ mmienu; Tendai Biti ne Awuraa Lynett Karenyi Kore; ɔkyerɛwfoɔ ma amamfrafoɔ nsɛm, Awura Gladys Hlatywayo; Ɔman Twerɛtwerɛfoɔ abɛdiakyire, Owura Lovemore Chinoputsa; ɔyɛ National Standing Committee muni, na ɔyɛ amanyɔkuo no kyerɛwfoɔ abɛdiakyire, David Chimhini ne Awuraa Vongai Tome.
Wɔahyɛ mmarima yi sɛ sɛ wɔkyere wɔn wie a, wɔntua dɔla apem wɔ ankorɛankorɛ biara akyi berɛ a akasakasa bi rekɔ so wɔ MDC Morgan Tsvangirai House no.
Awuraa Makwande kaa sɛ nnipa a wɔakyere wɔn no bɛsan akɔ kɔɔto wɔ Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so aduonu mmeɛnsa wɔ Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so aduonu mmeɛnsa wɔ Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so aduonu baako wɔ Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so aduonu baako wɔ Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so aduonu baako wɔ Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so aduonu baako wɔ Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so aduonu baako wɔ Kɔtɔnima da a ɛtɔ so aduonu baako wɔ Kɔtɔnima da a ɛt
Ɔne Studi 7 rekasa wɔ atɛnbuo no akyi no, mmaranimfoɔ nsia no mu baako, Alec Muchadeham kaa sɛ kɔɔto no hyɛɛ nnipa a wɔgyina wɔn ananmu no sɛ mma wɔnnsiw nhwehwɛmu no kwan.
Owura Muchadehama san kae sɛ ɛwom sɛ wɔbɔɔ nnipa baasia yi soboɔ wɔ nsɛmmɔne Mmara (Codification and Reform) ase deɛ, nanso wɔde nneduafoɔ a wɔde wɔn kɔɔ asɛnnibea anɔpa yi san kɔɔ polisifoɔ adwumam baabi a wɔbɔɔ wɔn soboɔ sɛ wɔato COVID-19 Prevention Act.
Mmaranimfoɔ nsia yi nso de asɛm no akɔdan kɔɔto wɔ nnipa a wɔde wɔn agu afiase no ho.
Owura Muchadehama kaa sɛ nnipa a wɔda afiase no nni ahobammɔ papa, enti sɛ wɔwɔ afiase a, wontumi nkyere wɔn anaa wɔmfa COVID-19 mma wɔn.

Awuraa Makwande akasa atia sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ amanyɔkuo no kasamafo abadiakyire Womberaishe Nhende a ɔda ayaresabea no gyina mmofra no mmonnaa.
Wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ Owura Nhende pirae Nnɛra bere a wɔkyeree no de no kɔɔ ayaresabea no.
Wɔ kɔkɔbɔ foforɔ mu no, Zimbabwe Mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ a ɔhwɛ Hokwan Ahorow a Nnipa wɔ so kyerɛ sɛ, wɔkyeree obi a ɔyɛ Polisini bere a ɔde Ɔmanpanin Emmerson Mnangagwa totoo kɔndɔm bi ho no, wɔde too dwa sɛ wɔde sika a ɛyɛ dɔla 300 na agyae no.
Asɛnnibea no bɛdi ɔsraani a ɔda sukuu no ano, Shungudzemoyo Kache nso asɛm wɔ ne fie.
Nkɔmhyɛ kwankyerɛfoɔ a ɔda Nkɔmhyɛ Ayaresa ne Nkwagye (P HD) Asoeɛ ano, Walter Magaya aka sɛ ɔne aman foforɔ reyɛ adwuma sɛ ɔbɛtu Aguma aduro a ɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔde sa HIV / AIDS, kokoram ne nea ɛkeka ho.
Berɛ a ɔne Studi7 rekasa wɔ mpaebɔ dwumadie bi a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Francistown, Botswana Wukuada anadwo no, Owura Magaya kaa sɛ ɔmpɛ sɛ ɔbɛyɛ n'adwene sɛ polisifoɔ bɛkyere no wɔ November 2018 mu bere a ɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ wanya HIV / AIDS ano aduro no.
Bere a Owura Magaya srɛɛ bɔne fafiri wɔ HIV / AIDS ho no, wɔbɔɔ no ka $ 700 wɔ February mu afe a etwaam no.
Nanso asɛm no ansiw Owura Magaya a ɔka kyerɛɛ Studio7 sɛ wɔne aman foforo a wɔmpɛ sɛ wɔbɔ din no reyɛ adwuma na ɔkaa sɛ wohuu Aguma ano aduru sɛ ɛyɛ HIV / AIDS yareɛ no ano aduru.
Owura Magaya kaa sɛ HIV / AIDS yareɛ no yɛ yareɛ a ɛwɔ Africa nti ɔhyɛɛ aman nyinaa sɛ wɔn nyinaa mmom nyɛ adwuma mfa mpɛ ɔhaw no ano aduru.
Owura Magaya kaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔne aman foforɔ yɛ adwuma, efisɛ na Zimbabwe nni ahotosoɔ sɛ nnuro no bɛsa ɔman no yareɛ a ɛdi awu no.
Nanso, wɔ asɛm a wɔde baa Magaya a ɛwɔ Zimbabwe so no, wohui sɛ Aretha Medical Company adwumakuw no nni din wɔ Zimbabwe Medical Control Authority mu, na wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ sɛ Apɔmuden Adwumayɛfoɔ no nhyɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnyɛ nhwehwɛmu nhu sɛ ebia Aguma aduru no yɛ adwuma anaa.
Dɔkota bi a ɔwɔ Francistown ayaresabea, Sengaphi Khuzwayo kasa tiaa Magaya sɛ ɔkae sɛ ɔrehwehwɛ sika.
Bere bi a atwam no na Owura Magaya ama akasakasa asɔre wɔ ɔman no mu bere a wɔkyeree no sɛ ɔtoo ɔbea foforo mmonnaa no, nanso akyiri yi kɔɔto guu asɛm no mu bere a wɔn a wɔde asɛm no kɔɔto guu asɛm no so mmara kwan so no.
Mmofra nnuruyɛfoɔ a wɔnni aban ayaresabea ahodoɔ no ama apemfoɔ nkwa da asiane mu sɛ wɔwɔ ɔhaw a ɛte sɛ nea ɛwɔ Chinhoyi Ayaresabea Kɛseɛ no.
Awuraa Lisa Sibanda yɛ ɔbea a wanya awo akyi adwenemhaw.
Awuraa Sibanda kae sɛ ne ba a na ɔda so ara mmofra no wuu wɔ yafunu mu bere a wɔde no maa no Benada no, nanso dɔkota biara antumi ammoa no kae sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔma ɔyarehwɛfo bi boa no ma owu.
Awuraa Sibanda se ɔhaw a ɛsen biara ne sɛ wɔbɛhohoro wɔn ntini mu ntɛm sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ebetumi apira wɔn.
Awuraa Sibanda se wɔn nso nsu ho ayɛ wɔn den, na wɔn nsa renka ayaresabea tiafidan ahorow no, na wɔregye nsu dedaw.

Zindoga kae sɛ wafa kar firi Kariba kɔ Chinhoyi wɔ kilomita aduonu num no ho ka efisɛ na nneɛma nkɔ yiye wɔ Kariba ayaresabea hɔ.

Cancer Association of Zimbabwe hyɛ ɔmanfoɔ nkuran sɛ wɔmpɛɛpɛɛ wɔn mu wɔ nufu mu kokoram ho ntɛm ansa na yareɛ no mu ayɛ den.
Wɔ Zimbabwe no, nnipa bɛboro 5,000 na wonya kokoram afe biara, nanso wɔn mu dodow no ara hu mmofra dɔkota wɔ yare a emu yɛ den yi ho.
Ahyehyɛde no panin, Junior Mavhu se mprempren wɔayɛ wɔn adwene sɛ wɔbɛhwehwɛ mmea ne mmarima mu wɔ nufu mu kokoram ho sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi ahwehwɛ mmoa bere ano.
Wɔka sɛ kokoram kunkum nnipa pii wɔ ɔman no mu, titiriw mmea, ɛwom sɛ ɛtaa yɛ mmarima de.
Cancer Center foforo rehyɛ mmea ne mmarima nkuran sɛ wɔmfa hokwan no nyɛ nhwehwɛmu wɔ October mu wɔ kokoram ho, na wɔnkyerɛkyerɛ wɔn yare no ho ade wɔ petee mu bere a wɔredi Wiase Nufu mu Kokoram Ɔsram no.
Wiase no rehwɛ ɔsram yi kwan sɛ ɛbɛkae nnipa sɛ wonim nufu mu kokoram ne ɔkwan a wobetumi afa so anya mu mfaso.
Awuraa Mavhu nyansahyɛ ne sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔhwɛ obiara anim daa sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi asa yare no na wɔasa no yiye ansa na atrɛw.

Nnipakum yi kɔɔ so wɔ wiase afanan nyinaa berɛ a na nsɛntwerɛfoɔ a wofi aman ahodoɔ so a wɔwɔ Zimbabwe rehwɛ abatoɔ a ɛdi kan ama Zanu PF kannifo Emmerson Mnangagwa, na na ɔredi ahurusi sɛ ɔbɛyɛ ɔmanpanin wɔ amanyɔkuo no kan ɔmampanyin Robert Mugabe a watwa mu no akyi.
Na Mnangagwa retu mmirika atia Nelson Chamisa a ɔyɛ MDC Apam no kannifo, a na amanyɔkuo nketewa a wɔyɛ ɔsɔretiafo ka ho.
Wɔ atuo a wɔtotowee no akyi no, wɔhyɛɛ aban no ma ɔhyehyɛɛ adwumakuo a wɔde bɛyɛ nhwehwɛmu. Saa adwumakuo yi maa kan South Africa ɔmanpanin Kgalema Motlanthe bɛyɛɛ ne guamtenani.
Asoeɛ no de asɛm bi too dwa a ɛkyerɛ sɛ asraafoɔ ne polisifoɔ akum nnipa nsia no, na wɔka kyerɛɛ wɔn sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde awudifoɔ no ba atɛntenenee mu. Ɛsan nso hyɛɛ aban sɛ ɔmma wɔn abusuafoɔ ka.
Owura Motlanthe asoeɛ nso kaa sɛ aban mma nea wawu no mma nkɔ sukuu, na sɛ nkurɔfo sɔre tia polisifoɔ ne asraafoɔ a wɔmfa mmara no nhyɛ wɔn nsa.
Abenfo a wɔhwehwɛ nnipa kyɛfa ho nsɛm ka sɛ aban nnyee ne ho ase mmaa Motlanthe Commission no.

Asoafoɔ no mu baako a ɔkyerɛw amanneɛbɔ no, Lovemore Madhuku, a ɔno nso yɛ Ɔman Mmara Kwan so Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie guamtenani no kaa sɛ n’adwuma no awieɛ n'adwuma no, na ɛyɛ Mnangagwa aban no asɛm sɛ ɔbɛhwɛ ama wɔadi saa ahyɛdeɛ no so.
Madhuku nso kaa sɛ n’adwumakuo ahyɛ aban sɛ ɔmfa asraafoɔ ne polisifoɔ a wɔabɔ wɔn tuo no mmɛtua wɔn abusuafoɔ ka.
Hokwan a nnipa wɔ ho nimdefo ne Hokwan a Nnipa wɔ ho kwankyerɛfoɔ a ɔda North Africa mantam mu, Dewa Mavhinga se aban no nkyerɛ sɛ n’ani gye ho sɛ ɔde Motlanthe Commission Report no bɛdi dwuma.
Mavhinga kaa sɛ adi mfeɛ mmienu fi bere a wɔde amanneɛbɔ no too dwa, nanso sɛdeɛ Motlanthe adwumakuo no kamfo kyerɛɛ no, wɔnkyeree ɔsraani biara.
Mmeae pii wɔ hɔ a wɔatu akwan bere a ɔmanpanin Emmerson Memangagwa, n’asomfo, mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu nnipa ne adwadifoɔ de wɔn ho bɔɔ ɔmanfoɔ ho sɛ wɔbɛsiesie wɔn adwumayɛbea na wɔatena Ɔman Ahotew Dwumadie a ɛbaa asram abiɛsa a atwa mu no ase.
Mnangagwa ne n’asomfo a wɔboa siesiee ayaresabea hɔ tebea a ɛho ntew no kɔɔ Parirenyatwa Ayaresabea anɔpatutuutu.
Ɔrekasa wɔ ayaresabea hɔ sɛ wɔasiesie hɔ no, Owura Mnangagwa kaa sɛ wɔagye dwumadie no atom yiye, na ɛyɛ dwumadie pa a ɛbɛma nnipa akwahosan atu mpɔn.
Ɔkaa sɛ wahyehyɛ da no sɛ ɔkwan a ɔnam so bɛkae nkurɔfo sɛ yei ne ade a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ no da biara.
Owura Mnangagwa san kae sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ nnipa yi nwura a wɔtow gu no gu, na wosua biribi fi aman bi te sɛ Rwanda a wɔmma nnipa kwan mma wɔnnwene afie ne sare so anaa wɔnnantew sɛnea wɔn nan te so.
Agumadi Soafoɔ, Kirsty Coventry ne n’adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔhyɛɛ aseɛ tuu kwan wɔ Simon Muzenda Street na wɔde wɔn kɔɔ Africa Unity Square kɔkaa Meikles Hotel ne TM Supermarket adwumayɛfoɔ ho.
Wɔkae sɛ ɔmanfo ho dwiriw wɔn sɛ wohuu wɔn wɔ abɔnten so, na ɛsɛ sɛ nkurɔfo siesie wɔn mpɔtam hɔ bere nyinaa.
Adwumayɛfoɔ a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ Zimbabwe atesɛm nkrataa mu nso akɔ akwan a ɛwɔ adwumakuo no adwumayɛbea ti hɔ so, na adwumakuo no nso atɔ bosea de akɔhyɛ mmɔnten so sɛ wɔmfa nwura ngu hɔ.
Zimpapers kasamafo Beatrice Tonhodzayi ka kyerɛɛ Studio 7 sɛ efĩ abu so wɔ mpɔtam a wɔyɛ adwuma no araa ma wɔahu sɛ ɛfata sɛ wɔne aban yɛ adwuma de siesie kurow no ne ɔman no.

Dapɛn a etwaam no, wɔtew atua a ɛhwehwɛ sɛ wɔkyerɛkyerɛ wɔn mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ a wɔayi wɔn afi afiase hɔ no mu.
Wɔayɛ nhyiamu sɛ mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ ne IFP mansini mu mpaninfoɔ nyinaa mfa mmuaeɛ mma ɔmanfoɔ.
“Ɔhaw no fii ase berɛ a na ɔmanfoɔ bi gyina asa no akyi, na berɛ a nhyiamu no hyɛɛ aseɛ no, wosiw kwan a ɛbɛn asa no, wɔhyehyɛɛ aboɔ wɔ banbɔfoɔ mu na wɔhyɛɛ wɔn ma wɔtoo tuo esiane sɛ na ɔmanfoɔ no reba wɔn so nti.
Ɔkae sɛ na ɔmanfo no bi kura atuo.
Wɔn a wɔbaa nhyiamu yi ase ne kurow sohwɛfo foforo a wɔato nsa afrɛ no biologela, ne mmarahyɛbɛdwani ntombela ne mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ a wɔwɔ Mthonjaneni Mansini mu.
Mmɔden a wɔbɔe sɛ wobegye mmuae afi ɔmantam no kannifo hɔ no anyɛ yiye efisɛ wotumi gyee wɔn ahunmu nsrahwɛ no mu na wɔantumi annya mmuae.
Mansini no kasamafoɔ, Thami Shangase kaa sɛ ɛnyɛ Mansini no na ɔyɛɛ saa nhyiamu yi ho nhyehyɛeɛ, na ɔde kaa ho sɛ asɛm no yɛ polisifoɔ nsam.
IFP mankasamafoɔ a ɔda amanyɔkuo no ano, Mkholy Hlengwa kaa sɛ wɔde asɛm yi bɛto dwa ɛnnɛ.
Basabasayɛ hyɛɛ aseɛ berɛ a woyii biologela ( kan kurow sohwɛfoɔ) ne mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ nan fii hɔ, na ɛde mpaapaemu baa ɔmanfoɔ mu, ne titiriw IFP mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ a ɔhwɛ ɔman no so.
KwaZulu-Natal polisi kasamafoɔ, Colonel Thembeka Mbele kaa sɛ wɔabue nsɛm a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ sɛ wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ sɛ wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ sɛ wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ sɛ wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ sɛ wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ wɔ Melmoth polisifoɔ adwumam.
Mbete nnye ntom sɛ ɔrebu n’ani agu kɛtɛasehyɛ ne porɔeɛ so
Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie Kasamafoɔ bi a wɔfrɛ no Baleka Mbethe abɔ soboɔ a ɛfa kɛtɛasehyɛ ne kɛtɛasehyɛ ho no agu, na waka sɛ emu bi yɛ akyinnyegyeɛ.
Awuraa Mbete a ɔrema nsɛmmisa a efi asoeɛ bi a wɔyɛ nhwehwɛmu wɔ aban nkɛntɛnso mu a wɔn mu kakraa bi na wɔrebua, a ɔkyerɛ sɛ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie mu nnipa bi na wɔde wɔn ho ahyɛ dwowtwa mu no kaa sɛ nsɛm bi wɔ hɔ a ntease nni saa soboɔ yi mu, na afoforo nso de, ɛte sɛ nea nnipa a wɔwɔ nimdeɛ nni adanse biara a ɛkyerɛ sɛ wɔn tirim yɛ den.
Ɔtwee adwene sii akode ho ɔsɛmpɔw a ɛfa ɔmanpanin abɛdiakyire Jacob Zuma ho no so sɛ ɛyɛ nokwasɛm a ɛyɛ sɛ ne nsa kaa krataa bi a ɛkyerɛkyerɛ nsɛm a emu yɛ den mu nanso na onnim onii a ɔde bae.
"Asoafoɔ panin, minim nnipa bi a wɔadi adanseɛ wɔ ha, ne ɔkwan a Huawei no nam so retu mmirika no.
Minim nso sɛ ɔkasafo no aba ha na ɔkae sɛ ɛnyɛ nea wotee no kɛkɛ na mubetumi aka.
"Mɛtumi aka nsa ano asɛm, asɛm a wɔde too dwa (Mondada) no.
Wɔde krataa bi ahyɛ me dwumadibea pon ase.
Na nsɛm a ɛyɛ ahodwiriw na ɛyɛ ahodwiriw wɔ krataa no mu nanso wɔamfa ne nsa anhyɛ ase na obiara ankyerɛw.
Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie nni adagyew koraa, mintumi nnye saa nhoma yi bere a minhu nea ɔkyerɛwee na yɛkaa ho asɛm.
Ɔhaw no ne nea ɔkyerɛwee no, na ɛsɛ sɛ saa nipa no ba me nkyɛn bɛte me ase.
Merebɔ mmɔden sɛ mɛma mmuaeɛ seesei sɛ yɛwɔ Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie a yɛrentumi nka nsɛm a ɛrekɔ so no.
Wɔ June 2017 mu no wobisaa no nea na ɔreyɛ wɔ Gupta abusua asɛm bi mu.
"Merenkae yiye de, nanso minim sɛ nsɛm a ɛresisi no reka Guptasfo no.
Misusuw sɛ ansa na saa nsɛm no bɛba no, na yɛafrɛ wɔn a wɔkyerɛwee no.
Ma yɛnhwɛ nea wɔka fa wiase a atwa wo ho ahyia no ho.
“Sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yebetumi anya nkyerɛkyerɛmu na yɛatumi ayɛ yɛn adwuma no, Awuraa Mbethe na ɔtoo nsa frɛɛ no.
Wɔbɔɔ NSFAS sobo sɛ wama osuani bi awu
ADESUAFOɔ rebɔ NSFAS soboɔ wɔ sukuuni bi a ɔdii nna mmienu wɔ sukuu no abɔnten a ɛwɔ Durban Tvet Kɔlege a ɛwɔ Cato Manor Memeneda no wuo ho.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ nnipa a ɔte hɔ no yii nea wawu no, Yonwabo Manyanya(26), a wawie anyinam ahoɔden mfidie Adansi adwuma no fii hɔ esiane ɛka a wɔde tuaa ho ka nti.
Wɔhyɛɛ nea wawu no ma ɔdaa abɔnten nnanu efisɛ na onni baabiara a ɔde sie bere a woyii no fii ne fie Dwoda no.
Wɔbɔɔ amanneɛ Wukuada sɛ na nea wawu no nni apɔwmuden.
Wɔbɔ amanneɛ sɛ ne mfɛfo sukuufo no ka kyerɛɛ no sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔhwehwɛ baabi a ɔde sie.
Amanneɛbɔ kyerɛ sɛ Yonwabo a wɔkyerɛ sɛ ɔte mpɔtam hɔ no wuui Memenda wɔ baabi a na n’adamfo no te wɔ Durban Atifi fam no.
Asuafoɔ no mu baako a na ɔbɛn nea wawu no paa na ɔsrɛɛ sɛ mma wɔmmɔ ne din no kaa sɛ nea esiiɛ no maa wɔn ho dwirii wɔn, na ɔkasa tiaa NSFAS sɛ wɔatwe wɔn nan agye sika.
"M’ani nnye wɔ asɛm yi akyi.
Mepɛ sɛ NSFAS de ne ho gye nsɛm mu efisɛ ɛte sɛ nea nsɛm a ɛresisi pii bɛba saa bere a awɔw bere rekɔ so wɔ sukuu no mu no.
Nea wawu no busuani bi a na ontumi nka ne ho asɛm nkyerɛ nsɛmtwerɛfoɔ.
KwaZulu-Natal polisi kasamafoɔ Panyin Nqobile Gwala kaa sɛ asɛm biara nsiiɛ.
Sikasɛm mu ahokyere no atrɛ akɔ kɔlege a ɛwɔ Asherville sukuu mu wɔ Sydenham, bere a asuafoɔ bɛboro 50 tew atua wɔ abɔnten apon no ano nnɛ no.
Asuafoɔ no ka kyerɛɛ Isolered sɛ wɔada ɔkwan a ɛda mfinimfini hɔ no akyi, efisɛ wɔatwa wɔn afi wɔn dan a wɔnnye ho akatua no mu.
Asuafo no mu dodow no ara a na wɔhyɛ pajamas no firi akyirikyiri te sɛ Gauteng, Eastern Cape ne Mpum Shanghai.

"Duan ho sika biara nni hɔ.
Wɔde akwantu ho ka ne sika ketewaa bi a wogye maa adesrɛfoɔ.

Zimbabwe Asɔre Asoeɛ (ZCC) se Matabeleland Kesee fam, Matabeleland Atifi ne Bulawayo mansini no suahu berɛ a wɔde ntamasin a ahobammɔ wom rema ayarehwɛfoɔ a wɔyɛ adwuma wɔ asɔre ayaresabea ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ mantam no mu no ama wɔn werɛ ahow yie.

Nanso wɔne mpanyimfoɔ a wɔwɔ Zimbabwe Ayaresabea Nnuruyɛfoɔ Nkabomkuo mu, Dr. Elias Muzoremba yɛɛ nhyiamu sɛ wɔrekasa atia dɔkotafoɔ no.
Wɔ krataa a dɔkotafoɔ no kyerɛw kɔmaa nsɛntwerɛfoɔ mu no, wɔka kyerɛɛ ɔmanpanin no adwumayɛbea sɛ Apɔmuden Asoeɛ no redaadaa wɔn.
Nnuruyɛfoɔ no se wɔpɛ sɛ aban di ɔhaw a ɛfa nnubɔne ho dwuma wɔ ayaresabea ahodoɔ ne adwumayɛbea foforɔ na ɔde US dɔla ma wɔn sɛdeɛ ɔde retwɛn RTGS.
Seesei dɔkotafoɔ yi nya dɔla 329 ɔsram biara. Nanso saa sika yi wɔ RTGS mu.
Nanso sikasɛm ho ɔbenfo bi a ɔwɔ Nelson Mandela Metropolitan University, Professor Gift Mugano ka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ aban ntumi ntɔ sika no koraa.
Yɛsan nso bisaa Dr Mugano ɔkwan bɛn so na nnwuma bi regye US dollars wɔ wɔn nneɛma ho, ɔkwan bɛn so na ɛbɛtumi atu mpɔn?
Ɔpanyin a ɔda Community Working Group on Health ano, Owura Itai Rusike, ka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ ɛho hia sɛ aban ma apɔmuden nnwuma sika pii wɔ sikasɛm mu.
Nnipa pii a wɔwɔ ɔman no mu nso rebɔ wɔn soboɔ sɛ Health Insurance card no nyɛ adwuma, na sɛ wɔtɔ nnuro a, wɔka kyerɛ wɔn sɛ wɔmfa US dɔla mma wɔn fie sɛdeɛ wɔpɛ.
Ɔman bɔɔlbɔkuo a wɔyɛ akofoɔ yi agyaw wɔn akɔ South Africa akɔ kofa.
Ekuo no hyia akasakasa mmienu wɔ Cosafa cup no ne Africa Nations cup no mu a ɛsɛ sɛ wɔhyɛ aseɛ wɔ Cosafa cup no mu Memeneda no.
Nea ɛka ho ne sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ wɔde kofa bɔɔlbɔkuo no siesie wɔn ho ma Afcon no, ɛwɔ sɛ wɔsan gyina nkonta a ɛtɔ so nsia wɔ afe a atwa mu no akyi, sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛhyɛ din pa a wɔwɔ sɛ Atifi fam bɔɔlbɔkuo no mu kena afe yi.
Esiane sikasɛm mu ahokyere nti, Zimbabwe ntumi nhwehwɛ akuw a wɔbɛdeda wɔn a wɔn ho akokwaw ansa na Afcon reba ne akofoɔ a wɔyɛ akofoɔ bɔɔlbɔkuo Sunday Chifambwa se, Cosafa ne ɔkwan koro pɛ a ɔbɛfa so ahyɛ n’asraafoɔ no den.
Chidzambwa nso rehwɛ kwan sɛ ɔbɛma din pa a ɔwɔ wɔ Cosafa agodie no mu ayɛ kɛse bere a ɔbɛyɛɛ bɔɔlbɔkuo a odi kan a odii nkonim mprɛn nan fi bere a wɔhyɛɛ agodie no ase wɔ afe 1997 mu no.
Chidzambwa dii Cosafa cup no mu nkunim afe 2003, afe 2017 ne afe 2018 mu.
Zimbabwe bɔɔlbɔkuo foforɔ te sɛ Tendai Darikwa, Admiral Muskwe, ne Alec Mudimu nso pɛ sɛ wɔbɛdi dwuma wɔ Cosafa cup a wɔte nka sɛ wonnim no mu.
Afe yi, Zimbabwe wɔ bɔɔlbɔkuo a ɛwɔ ahoɔden sen biara wɔ agodie yi nyinaa mu berɛ a wɔn bɔɔlbɔkuo no de wɔn ani kyerɛɛ Afcon a bɔɔlbɔkuo foforɔ te sɛ Nimdeɛ Musona ne Marvelous Nakamba ka ho.
Zimbabwe Akofo Fan Club, Shingirai Miti, ka sɛ akansie biara nni hɔ ma Cosafa efisɛ nkontabuo no yɛ Zimbabwe de bere nyinaa.
Esiane sɛ akofoɔ no adi Cosafa cup no nti, wɔrehwɛ nea ɛdi kan wɔ Afcon agodie a wɔhyiaa Misraim wɔ wɔn bɔɔlbɔ a ɛdi kan no mu.
Bɔɔlbɔkuo no mu bɔɔlbɔni a yɛfrɛ no Ronald Pfumbidzai se wɔnkɔ Misraim nkɔka bɔɔlbɔkuo ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ hɔ no ho.
Zimbabwe ne Misraim, Democratic Republic of Congo ne Uganda na ɛwɔ Akuo A soafoɔ panin Wellington Mpandare wɔ ahotosoɔ sɛ ɔbɛfi hɔ.

Nanso afe yi mu no, berɛ a ebinom kɔsrasra wɔn abusuafo ne wɔn nnamfo afe baako akyi a wɔanhu wɔn ho wɔn ho no, FC Platinum bɔɔlbɔni a ɔkyerɛ agumadi no ho anisoɔ sɛdeɛ wɔwɔ Kairo, Misraim, berɛ a wɔne Al Ahly redi nsawɔsoɔ wɔ Caf Champions League mu no.
Yei bɛyɛ FC Platinum agumadi a ɛtɔ so abiɛsa wɔ akansi no mu, bere a Sudanni Al Hilal bɔɔ no 1 - 2 wɔ ne nan a edi kan mu, na ɔhweree 3 - 3 maa Tunisia Etoile duSahel.

ƆMAMPANYIN, Obert Masaraure se, sɛ bɔɔlbɔkufo no, wɔn nso pɛ asetra pa, nanso ɛnyɛ sɛnea wɔpɛ no na ɛbɛkɔ so.
Masaraure se ɛwom sɛ aban se ɔdwene sikasɛm ho de, nanso sɛ ɔko tia dwowtwa wɔ ne baa dwumadibea ahodoɔ, na ɔsan hwɛ ɔman no sikasɛm yie a, ebetumi ama nneɛma akɔ yie.
Masaraure se aban sika no fã kɛse no ara resɛe wɔ nnwuma a ɛho nhia te sɛ amamfrafo akwantu, kar insurance ne nneɛma foforo a wobetumi de asi hɔ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛma aban asomfo akatua pa.
Masaraure ka wɔ ne nsusuwii mu sɛ, sika wɔ ɔman no mu a ebetumi adi ɔhaw ahorow ho dwuma, nanso ɔhaw no ne sɛ wɔnhwɛ ɔman no toɔ so yiye, na wonhu hia a ɛho hia sɛ wosiesie nneɛma a aban mpanyimfo de ma wɔn no.
Aman foforɔ so amanfoɔ renwiinwii wɔ ɛka kɛseɛ a wɔbɔ wɔ akwantuo krataa a ɛrenya nkɔanim anaa apam ahodoɔ a ɛwɔ hɔ seisei no ho.

Ɔne nsɛmtwerɛfoɔ rekasa no, Ɔsoafoɔ Kazembe kaa sɛ n’adwumakuo no nim akwanhwɛ a ɛkorɔn a nnipa wɔ sɛ wɔn nsa bɛka wɔn akwantuo krataa ntɛm sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ yie ara, ne sɛ nnipa a ɛyɛ den sɛ wɔn nsa bɛka saa nkrataa yi, ɛnkanka amamfrafoɔ.
Kazembe kaa sɛ, sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ na amamfrafoɔ bɛnya mmara ho nkrataa wɔ wɔn man mu no, aban ahu sɛ ɛfata sɛ ɔma boɔ kɔ soro, na ɔde saa nkrataa yi bɛma wɔn ntɛm ara.
Nanso nnipa bi a wofi aman foforo so te nka sɛ aban afa saa anammɔntuo yi so ama amamfrafoɔ ntam nkitahodie akɔ so.
Sɛ wɔkyekyem pɛpɛɛpɛ a, obi a ɔwɔ passport wɔ ɔman no mu nya sika a ɛyɛ $ 53 wɔ RTGS ho, na nea ɔpɛ sɛ ofi adi wɔ nnansa mu no nya $ 250.

Isaac Nyaumba a ɔyɛ Zimbabweni no kae sɛ n’ani agye sɛ onyaa hokwan hyiaa bɔɔlbɔni bi a wagye din a wɔfrɛ no Neymar mfonini.
Neymar a wɔwoo no wɔ São Paulo, Brazil ne ne din ankasa ne Neymar da Silva Santos Júnior.
Seesei Neymar ne bɔɔlbɔni foforɔ a ɔno nso ne no redi agoru wɔ Spain bɔɔlbɔkuo a ɛwɔ Barcelona no mu. Ɔsan nso di agoru wɔ Brazil a ɔdii bɔɔlbɔkuo a ɛtɔ so 23 no anim kɔɔ sika kɔkɔɔ abasobɔ mu nea ɛdi kan wɔ Olimpik no mu.
Nanso ɛwom sɛ nnipa pii ka sɛ wɔyii Nyaumba ne Neymar mfonini no wɔ Victoria Aworoeɛ hɔ deɛ, nanso wɔka kyerɛɛ Studi 7 sɛ wɔgyee berɛ a na wɔreyɛ adwuma wɔ Ukutula Conservation Center a ɛbɛn Pretoria a ɛwɔ South Africa no.
Mmaa bɔɔlbɔkuo a wɔyɛ akofoɔ yi reko agoru kɛseɛ bi wɔ wɔn abakɔsɛm mu, a ɔmanfoɔ pɛ sɛ Zimbabwe di nkunim sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wɔbɛhyɛn ɔman no agodie mu.
Akofoɔ a wɔyɛ den no rekɔ Rufaro Agumadibea Kwasida wɔ wɔn akansi a ɛso paa firi mmerɛ a Zimbabwe hyɛɛ amanaman ntam akansi ase no mu.
Mmea bɔɔlbɔkuo no reko atia Cameroon nnipa a wɔyɛ akatakyie no wɔ bɔɔlbɔ mu a ɛbɛkyerɛ sɛ ebia Zimbabwe bɛfata ama afe a ɛreba Olimpik Agumadi wɔ Rio de Janeiro anaa ɛnyɛ saa.

Nanso aban nam Amanneɛbɔ Asoeɛ so de too dwa wɔ Twitter so sɛ polisifo asi mmabunu pii aboɔ.

Yɛntee asɛm no ho asɛm mfi polisifo hɔ.
Zimbabwe Community a ɛwɔ South Africa, ahyehyɛde a egyina Zimbabwefo a wɔte South Africa ne wɔn a wɔyɛ adwuma ananmu no se ɛhaw wɔn yiye wɔ korɔnobɔ nkɔso a ɛrekɔ so wɔ Johannesburg mmorɔn a wosusuw sɛ Zimbabwefo na wɔredi no ho.
Kuo no se nsɛmmɔne a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Hillbrow, Berea ne Yeoville no yɛ amamfrafoɔ bebree te sɛ wɔn a wɔkyere nkurɔfo sie, wɔn a wɔkyere nkurɔfo sie, wɔn a wowɔ wɔn sekan ne awudifoɔ.
Sɛnkyerɛnne kwankyerɛfoɔ a ɔwɔ Zimbabwe a ɛwɔ South Africa kaa sɛ na wɔayɛ wɔn adwene sɛ wɔbɛhyia polisifoɔ ama asɛm no akɔ so, na wɔahyɛ polisifoɔ nkuran sɛ wɔnyɛ biribi a anibere wom.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Bere a ɛtɔ so nsia a ɛbɛyɛ ɔsram a edi hɔ no, n’ahyehyɛde no rehwɛ kwan sɛ ɔne polisifo a wɔhwɛ mansini ahodoɔ so no bɛhyia ayɛ adwuma abɔ mu ayi ɔhaw no afiri hɔ.
Wɔsan ka sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ polisifo kyinkyin hɔ, nanso mpɛn pii no, wɔnni hɔ, na ɛno bɛma akorɔmfo ne akorɔmfo a wɔreyɛ Jojina adwuma no.
Owura Marko kaa sɛ nnipa a wɔhunuu amane yi mu bebree nim nnipa a wɔayɛ bɔne yi bi wɔ wɔn ankasa kasa mu, enti ɛwɔ sɛ polisifo a wɔayɛ krado sɛ wɔbɛyɛ bɔne no yɛ Zimbabwefo a wɔte saa mmeaeɛ yi mu adwuma.
