Ɔkaa sɛ asɛmmisa a ɔde kɔmaa Sikasɛm Soafoɔ Owura Ken Ofori-Attah no bɛboa ɔne Ghanafoɔ ma wɔahwehwɛ nsɛm foforɔ a ɛbɛboa nkɔmmɔ a ɛrekɔ so wɔ manfoɔ dwumadie mu afa ɔmanpanin de wimhyɛn akwantuo ho.
“Mede me nsa ahyɛ asɛmmisa yi ase nso sɛ mɛte ɛka a ɔman yi bɔe afe 2013 kosi 2017 ntam hɔ, berɛ a na kan Ɔmanpanin Mahama nam wimhyɛn akwantuo so retu kwan no”
Biribiara nni hɔ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ obi yɛ pɛ
Ɔrekyerɛkyerɛ n'atirimpɔw a ɛne sɛ ɔde asɛmmisa a egye ntɛmpɛ a mprempren ɛwɔ Kasamafoɔ Adwumayɛbea hɔ no mu no, Owura Barima kaa sɛ n’asɛmmisa no nni amanyɔsɛm ho adwene biara.
“Bɛyɛ mmerɛ a yɛsisii gyinaeɛ wɔ aban akwantuo nhyehyɛeɛ ho, na sɛ yɛhu nea ɛrekɔ so a, ɛnde yɛbɛtumi asi gyinaeɛ a ɛte saa ara.
Ɔkaa sɛ: “So biribi na ɛdii kan yɛɛ asɛm yi? Na sɛ biribi na ɛdii kan yɛɛ asɛm a, dɛn na ɔyɛe? Na so akwankyerɛ bi wɔ hɔ a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɔmampanyin akwantuo yi rekɔ so? Enti ɛda adi pefee sɛ mempɛ sɛ mɛyɛ amanyɔsɛm mu nsakraeɛ biara.”
Ɔde kaa ho sɛ: “Mepɛ sɛ yɛyɛ akyinnyegyeɛ ne ɔkasa a ɛfata sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a yɛbɛtumi akyerɛkyerɛ nsɛm mu yiye. Ɛnnɛ, ɛbɛtumi ayɛ m’aban, nanso ɔkyena ɛbɛyɛ obiara aban, enti sɛ yɛanhwehwɛ nkyerɛkyerɛmu a ɛfata na yɛanhwie akwantuo a ɛtete sɛɛɛ yi mma awieɛ a, yɛbɛhu sɛ yɛwɔ saa tebea yi mu berɛ nyinaa.”
Ablakwa asɛmmisa a ɛho hia
Ananmusini a ɔda amamfrafoɔ nsɛm ho Dwumadie ano, Owura Samuel Okudzeto Ablakwa nso de asɛmmisa bi a ɛho hia too Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie anim sɛ aban no nkyerɛkyerɛ nea enti a Ɔmanpanin Nana Addo Dankwa Akuffo-Addo amfa wimhyɛn annyɛ adwuma wɔ France nnansa yi.
Sɛdeɛ National Democratic Congress (NDC) North Tongu Member a ɔda Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie ano (MP) kyerɛ no, "Yei yɛ abufuw ne pɛsɛmenkominya a ɛyɛ sɛ Ghana bɛnya wimhyɛn papa a ɛyɛ adwuma pɛpɛɛpɛ" ne charter wimhyɛn a ɛyɛ adwuma sɛ ɔmampanyin.”
Ɔsan nso buu akontaa sɛ Ɔmanpanin akwantuo no boɔ boro GH ɔpepem mmienu.
Bono East Mantam soafoɔ, Owura Kwasi Adu-Gyan akamfo New Patriotic Party (NPP) ne National Democratic Congress (NDC) wɔ biakoyɛ a wɔayɛ ama asomdwoeɛ atena ɔmantam no mu.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “M’ani agye paa sɛ mahu sɛ NPP ne NDC a ɛwɔ Bono Apueɛ reyɛ adwuma abom asomdwoeɛ mu de asiesie akasakasa a ɛda wɔn ntam wɔ amanyɔsɛm mu”
Owura Adu-Gyan kaa sɛ asomdwoe na ɛmaa mpuntuo bɛnyaa nkɔsoɔ, na ɔkaa sɛ, sɛ asomdwoeɛ nni hɔ a, ɛbɛyɛ den sɛ mpuntuo bɛnya nkɔsoɔ wɔ mantam no mu.
Ɔmantam soafoɔ no de saa nkamfoɔ yi too dwa wɔ asɛm bi a ɔde too dwa wɔ nhyiamu bi a ɛkɔɔ so wɔ Techiman ase.
NPP ananmusifoɔ ne NDC ananmusifoɔ, aban mpanyimfoɔ, bammɔ nnwuma, Abatoɔ Asoeɛ (EC), National Commission or Civic Education (NCCE) ne ɔmanfoɔ fekuw (CSO) na wɔbaa dwumadie no ase.
Na nhyiamu a Ɔman Asomdwoeɛ Bagua no hyehyɛeɛ a efi Commonwealth Secretariat hɔ no asɛmti ne: “Countering Post 2020 Abatoɔ Violence, and Building Consensus for Greater Political Tolerance in Ghana”
Nsɛmti a wosusuw ho no fa ɔkwan a wɔfa so siesie abatoɔ mu basabasayɛ ne anwiinwii ne akasakasa a ɛkɔfa abatoɔ mu ba no ho.
Owura Adu-Gyan kaa sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ Ghanafoɔ ma ɔman no hoahoa wɔn ho sɛ wiase nyinaa asomdwoeɛ ho akontabuo a ɛtɔ so mmienu wɔ Africa no, na ɔkyerɛɛ hia a ɛho hia sɛ NPP ne NDC bɛbom aboa ama asomdwoeɛ a ɛrekɔ so wɔ ɔman no mu no mu ayɛ den.
Ɔkaa sɛ, “Yei yɛ ahemfoɔ, amanyɔkuo ahodoɔ, banbɔ nnwuma, ne mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ, mmarahyɛbɛdwafoɔ, atɛnmuaeɛ ne nsɛmtwerɛfoɔ”
Ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ Ɔmantam Nkitahodie Bagua no bɛhwɛ ama asomdwoeɛ a ɛho hia na ama mpuntuo aba mu.
Wɔ abatoɔ atɛntenenee mu no, Ɔkyerɛkyerɛfoɔ Panin a ɔda Bono Mantam Asomdwoeɛ Bagua ano, Alhaji Suallah Abdallah Quandah kaa sɛ abatoɔ atɛntenenee dii dwuma titiriw wɔ amanyɔsɛm nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛwɔ ɔman no mu no mu.
Ɔkyerɛkyerɛɛ mu sɛ abatoɔ mu atɛntenenee yɛ adeɛ a ɛho hia paa a ɛmfa ho sɛ ɛnyɛ adeɛ foforɔ no, wɔagye atom sɛ abatoɔ mu atɛntenenee yɛ adeɛ a ɛho hia paa a ɛbɛsi amanyɔsɛm ne abatoɔ mu basabasayɛ ano.
Ɔtwee adwene sii hia a ɛho hia sɛ wɔyɛ ɔman no abatoɔ atɛntenenee nhyehyɛeɛ mu mpɛnsɛmpɛnsɛmpɛnsɛ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a ɛbɛwie n'adwuma a ɛne sɛ wɔbɛma abatoɔ akɔ so pɛpɛɛpɛ na nteaseɛ wɔ mu no so.
Abuakwa South Mmarahyɛbɛdwani Samuel Atta Akyea ahyɛ Ghanafoɔ bɔ sɛ Nana Akuffo-Addo aban bɛsiesie wɔn ntam bere a NPP bɛdi tumi afe a ɛtɔ so aduonu mmeɛnsa wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu.
Sɛdeɛ ɔkyerɛ no, Ghanafoɔ benya sikasɛm mu ahofadi wɔ Nana Akufo-Addo akanni ase esiane sikasɛm nhyehyɛeɛ a nyansa wom a wɔbɛyi afi hɔ nti.
“Bere a ɛtɔ so nson no bɛyɛ berɛ foforɔ a ɛbɛma yɛadi yie na yɛanya fahodie, ne titiriw no sikasɛm mu ahofadi a Ghanafoɔ rehwehwɛ no. Ghanafoɔ bɛhu sɛ Onyankopɔn agye ɔman no afiri ahokyereɛ mu,” Atta Akyea kaa wɔ ntoboa bi a ɔde maa Asiakwa SOS a ɛwɔ Akim Apueɛ Mantam mu.
Ɔkae sɛ wasiesie ne ho sɛ ɔbɛsom sɛ asafo mu panin, sɛ Ɔmanpanin Nana Akufo-Addo bɛma no bi a.
Nneɛma a ɔde kɔe no bi ne ɛmo kotoku ason, anwa, nkyene, asikre, nufusu, nsa ne sika a wɔnka ho asɛm.
Wɔahu anuanom mmea mmiɛnsa bi a wɔda wɔn maame asanomfie wɔ Tarkwa-Nsuta a ɛwɔ Tarkwa-Nsuaem mansini a ɛwɔ Atɔeɛ Mantam mu.
Nnipa baasa no wuui bere a wɔhomee wusiw fii generator bi mu no.
Panin Inspector George Sekyi a ɔwɔ Tarkwa-Nsuta keteke gyinabea kae sɛ wɔtoo nsa frɛɛ no December 18, sɛ mmofra baasa awuwu wɔ baabi a wɔnom nsa.
Ɔkaa sɛ ɔne n’asraafoɔ no de ahoɔhare kɔɔ hɔ nanso wɔka kyerɛɛ no sɛ wɔde ɔbaa a wawu no, Abena Amos, 15, Arabi Dadzi, 13 ne Akaba Dadzi, a wadi mfeɛ aduonu mmeɛnsa na wahyɛ no agyinaeɛ wɔ Tarkwa Aban Ayaresabea Morgue retwɛn sɛ wɔbɛyɛ no nhwehwɛmu.
Wɔ Starr News anototoɔ mu no, Emmanuel Ohene Gyan Owura Sekyi kaa sɛ wawu no ne wɔn maame a ɔyɛ adwuma wɔ baabi a wɔnom nsa wɔ Tarkwa Nsuem mantam mu no na na ɛte.
Ɔkae sɛ wosii gyinae sɛ wobetwa anadwo wɔ asanombea hɔ bere a wɔboaa wɔn maame ma ɔtɔn nsa no.
Adwumayɛbea hɔ panin no kae sɛ bosome da a ɛtɔ so dunson no anyinam ahoɔden dwumadie bi sii hɔ esiane osu kɛse bi a ɛtɔeɛ na ɛnam so maa Maame Dadzi de generator hyɛɛ adwumayɛbea hɔ sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a nea wawu no bɛnya hann bere a ɔda no. Akyire yi mmeawa no maame hui sɛ wɔawuwu bere a ɔkɔɔ adwumayɛbea hɔ anɔpa no.
Polisifo a wɔwɔ mpɔtam hɔ reyɛ nhwehwɛmu wɔ saa asɛm yi ho.
Ɔnokwafoɔ a ɔda National Democratic Congress ano, John Mahama se ɔbɛtoa Menzgold Nana Appiah Mensah panin a wagye din sɛ wɔfrɛ no NAM 1, no so ayi adwadifoɔ a wɔde wɔn sika ahyɛ wɔn nsa sɛ ɔbɛdi nkonim wɔ December nhwehwɛmu no mu.
Bere a ɔrekasa wɔ Tarkwa-Nsuaem a ɛwɔ Atɔeɛ Mantam mu no, na Owura Mahama nnim nea enti a Akufo-Addo aban no ani nnye ho sɛ ɔbɛgye din 1 agyapadeɛ na mmom ɔde wɔn abufuw bɛhyɛ adetɔfoɔ nsa.
“Dɛn na ɛyɛ soronko wɔ edin 1 no ho araa ma Akufo-Addo rebɔ ne ho ban? Dɛn nti na wode polisifo gu adetɔfo a wɔn ho nni asɛm so na edin 1 no nantew kwa”
Ɔhyɛɛ bɔ sɛ n’aban a edi hɔ no bɛhwehwɛ din no ne akwankyerɛfoɔ no mu yie na ɔde ɔkwampa biara a ɔbɛfa so agye sika no.
Ɔtenaa nkran Circuit Court a ɛwɔ Nkran a ɛyɛ Ɔhotefo Ellen Asamoah na ɔdi anim, na ɔtenaa atɛmmuo a Menzgold panin (CEO) a ɔyɛ Nana Appiah Mensah (NAM) atwa mu akɔsi October 1, 2020 mu.
Ná Ɔman no adi kan de soboɔ foforɔ aba Nkran Circuit Court mu Ayɛwohomumɔ da a ɛtɔ so aduonu mmeɛnsa wɔ 2020 mu.
Ɔpanyin abɛdiakyire a ɔda Polisi ano (ASP) Sylvester Asare ka kyerɛɛ Kɔɔto no sɛ n’akwankyerɛ ne sɛ ɔnkɔ so nni soboɔ foforɔ yi so na ɔntwe wɔn a wɔabɔ no soboɔ no aso.
Wɔ July 20 no, ASP Asare ka kyerɛɛ kɔɔto no sɛ, wɔreyɛ adwumaden de atu kɔɔto no fo wɔ asɛm no ho.
Ne saa nti, ɔbɔɔ kɔɔto no mpae sɛ ɔmma wɔn kwan tenten sɛnea ɛbɛyɛ a wobetumi atu kɔɔto no fo wɔ wɔn adwene wɔ asɛm no ho.
Ɔkae sɛ sɛ wɔde afotu no ma a, wɔbɛka akyerɛ wɔn a wɔabɔ wɔn sobo no sɛ wɔnkɔ kɔɔto nkɔyɛ nea ɛho hia.
Nanso Dwoada wɔ asɛnnibea no, kwaadubɔni no bɔɔ mpae sɛ wɔmma no kwan na ɔpenee so.
Na nea wɔabɔ no sobo no din 1 no wɔ asɛnnibea hɔ.
Circuit Court wɔ Ayɛwohomumɔ da a ɛtɔ so aduonu nsia wɔ afe mpem mmienu ne aduonu baako mu no wɔmaa no bail 1 a ne boɔ yɛ GH ɔpepepem baako a ɛwɔ nkyemu nnum, abiɛsa a ɛwɔ sɛ ɛfata.
Ɔsrɛɛ wɔn sɛ wɔnnyɛɛ bɔne wɔ soboɔ 13 a Ɔman no bɔɔ wɔn no nyinaa ho. Efi saa bere no, ɔman no ayɛ nsakraeɛ wɔ nkrataa a wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ no mu a ɛnnya mmaeɛ.
Ɔwɔ nso sɛ ɔbɔ polisifo amanneɛ Wukuada biara ɛbɔ nɔn du.
Mfiase no, wɔbɔɔ no sobo sɛ wadi nsɛmmɔne, wadi nkontomposɛm, wadi adwuma bi a wɔmma ho Kwan, wɔtɔn fagudeɛ a wɔmma ho Kwan, wɔde wɔn ho to mmara so, na wɔhyehyɛ sika.
Wɔkyerɛ sɛ wɔn a wɔabɔ wɔn soboɔ yi agye sika ahodoɔ a ɛyɛ GH ɔpepem baako ne akyire ɔpepem baako.
Okada a wɔde di dwuma wɔ aguadi mu no regye adwinnwen kɛse.
Polisifo akyerɛ nso sɛ nsɛmmɔnedi, akwanhyia, ne karka ho mmara a ɛfa moto ho akɔ soro.
Akyinnye biara nni ho sɛ, Okada ahunahuna no regyae, na ɛsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ biribi titiriw bi de hyɛ ahotew dwumadie mu.
Yɛahyia ɔhaw a emu yɛ den wɔ Okada a yɛde bedi dwuma no ho mpɛn pii.
Ɛnnɛ, ɛda adi pefee sɛ ɔman no rehyia ɔhaw wɔ moto ne sakre a wɔde di dwuma, titiriw wɔ aguadi mu.
Afe 2012 mu no, Mmarahyɛbɛdwafie hyehyɛɛ mmara a ɛfa akwantuo ho wɔ ɔman no mu.
Nneɛma a ɛka ho bi ne Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan so Mmara Kwan a ɛkyerɛ sɛ ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔma tumi krataa sɛ wɔmfa moto a etua akwantufo ka.
Ɛmfa ho saa mmara yi, okada ne sakre abiɛsa (pragya) adi akwantu nhyehyɛe no so wɔ ɔman no mmeae pii.
Wɔ nkuraase no, okada ne Pragya nkutoo na wɔde tu kwan kɔ gua so, apɔmuden adwumayɛbea ne nkurow foforo mu, ne mmeae foforo.
Nnipa a wɔtete nkuropɔn mu fam no, wotumi hwɛ sakre so di lɔɔre akwantuo a emu yɛ duru no so.
Esiane sɛ sakre no bo nyɛ den nti, wotumi de tu kwan a ɛyɛ fɛ.
Afei nso, esiane sɛ wonni ɔmanfo akwantu nhyehyɛe papa biara nti, wɔn ho wɔ mfaso.
Nanso, nnipa pii kyi okada ne Pragya esiane ɔhaw a wɔde ba akwan so ne titiriw no obu a wonni mma karka ho mmara nti.
Akwanhyia ne awuwuawuwu a abu so wɔ Okada a wɔde di dwuma ɔkwammɔne so no nso haw adwene.
Nokwarem no, ahyehyɛde pii, a Ghana Medical Association ne National Road Safety Authority ka ho, ahwehwɛ sɛ wɔbɛbara wɔn dwumadi sɛ ɔkwan a wɔfa so tu kwan wɔ ɔman no mu.
Yei ahyɛ ɔman no mu ma wɔ ɛpo bruu mu.
Nea enti a ɛte saa ne sɛ, ɛmfa ho sɛ mmara wɔ hɔ a ɛbara dwuma a wɔde di dwuma wɔ aguadi mu no, ɛyɛ ade titiriw a ɛma Ghanafo pii ho tɔ wɔn.
Yɛn a yɛwɔ Daily Graphic mu no adwene yɛ yɛn sɛ ɛsɛ sɛ ɔman no de mmara no di dwuma yiye na wɔfa akwan a ɛfata sen biara a ɛbɛma ɔmanfoɔ anya wɔn ahiadeɛ.
Wɔ India sɛ nhwɛso no, Pragya yɛ ɔkwan titiriw a wɔfa so tu kwan nanso yɛntee anwiinwii ho asɛm sɛdeɛ yɛte wɔ Ghana no.
Ɛnde, dɛn na yebetumi asua afi India na yɛde aba yɛn nhyehyɛe yi mu?
Ɛsɛ sɛ yɛma ɛtra yɛn adwenem sɛ esiane sɛ nnipa a wonnya adwuma nyɛ no redɔɔso nti, wɔn a wɔyɛ okada ne sakre mmiɛnsa ho adwuma no bu no sɛ ɛyɛ baabi a wonya akatua pa ma wɔne wɔn mmusua.
Nanso mprempren, okadas ne pragyas yɛ ɔhaw ma yɛn a yɛwɔ Daily Graphic mu no gye di sɛ ɛdenam nkyerɛkyerɛ, mmara ne mmara a ɛfata a wɔhwɛ ma ɛyɛ adwuma so no, ɛwɔ sɛ adwumayɛfo no di so, sɛ wohu sɛ ɔman no ntumi nni wɔn akyi a.
Bere a wɔresusuw mmara anaa nhyehyɛe a ɛwɔ hɔ seesei ho no, adwumayɛfo ntetee, tumi krataa a wɔde ma nea ɔte pɔnkɔ so ne moto ne moto baesekre nyinaa, ne akwanhyia ho sikatua bɛyɛ nea ɛfata kɛse.
Esiane sɛ nhyehyɛeɛ a ɛte saa wɔ hɔ nti, ɛbɛyɛ mmerɛw ama Ghana Polisi Adwumakuo no sɛ wɔbɛhwɛ ama mmara ayɛ adwuma, na wɔadi moto ne moto baesekre ahodoɔ a wɔmfa nhyɛɛ mmara ase ne wɔn a wɔredi nsɛmmɔne nso ho dwuma.
Seisei deɛ, Ghanafoɔ adwene nhyia wɔ akwantuo akwan mmienu yi ho, efisɛ wɔn ho wɔ mfasoɔ na wɔn ho akyere wɔn.
Daily Graphic gyedi sɛ sɛ yɛpɛ sɛ yɛn akwan yɛ pɛ na yɛma yɛn akwantu nhyehyɛe tu mpɔn a, ɛnde ɛsɛ sɛ yɛde ntease kura abɛn no mu na yedi ɔhaw no ho dwuma mprempren anaa daapem.
Menkae da bi a mekaee no nnansa yi ara wɔ Ghana sen Fida a etwaam, Green Ghana da no.
Na eyi yɛ da a wɔhyɛɛ yɛn nyinaa nkuran sɛ yɛnkɔ ngu dua.
Efi bere a mesan baa Ghana mfeɛ aduonu a atwam ni na mibehuiɛ sɛ yɛn man no yɛ soronko koraa wɔ nea ɛwɔ Asase Ho Nsɛm Nhoma no mu ho no, na ɛno ne mmɔden a ɛsen biara a matumi ayɛ biribi de asiesie yɛn nsase bɔne no.
Asase ne fagudeɛ Asoeɛ no de aba ɔpepem nnum maa yɛn sɛ yɛnnua, na anigyeɛ bi wɔ hɔ a menhunuuɛ da.
Ɛbɛtumi aba sɛ Ghanafoɔ ahu sɛ adeɛ baako a ɛhia sɛ yɛde yɛn adwene si so sen biribi foforɔ biara ne ɔman a yɛfrɛ no Ghana no.
Ɛnyɛ ɔkwan kɛkɛ, sukuu a agugu mu, ayaresabea a mpa nka ho, sukuu mmofra a wonni kɔmputa ne me nantew da, ɔyare mmoawa a ɛsen biara mpo, nea ɛsɛ sɛ yɛn nyinaa nya na yɛn ho yeraw yɛn ne yɛn asase yi tebea, asase a ɛhweree ne kwae, nsubɔnten a ɛrehuruw, nea na ɛyɛ ɔsram a awɔw wom a ɛma ɔhyew ne ɛwo koraa no.
Menhwɛɛ Asase Ho Nkyerɛkyerɛ Nhoma a ɛwɔ yɛn sukuu mu nnɛ no, nanso minim sɛ Ghana man no su ahorow a ɛwɔ nhoma a mede dii dwuma wɔ sukuu mu no nte sɛ ɛnnɛyi Ghana.
Yɛda so ara ka kwaebirentuw ahorow ho asɛm, nanso ɛnyɛ saa na ɛte wɔ yɛn nsase so.
Yɛda so ara ka wuram mmoa ho asɛm nanso na wɔakyere wɔn na wɔagye wɔn atrae hɔ mfeɛ bebree ni.
Seesei kwaebirentuw ne nkekaboa yi ka yɛn kasa ho, na ɛnyɛ yɛn kasa ankasa.
Nneɛma a na yesusuw sɛ ɛyɛ kwae mu nneɛma mpo ada adi sɛ wɔagu ho fĩ wɔ sika kɔkɔɔ ne aduannuru foforo a na wɔrehwehwɛ no mu.
Ebia yɛn tebea ankasa too yɛn mu dodow no ara na merehwɛ kwan sɛ wɔn a wɔamfa wɔn ho anhyɛ mu no benya ntease pa nti a ɛnsɛ sɛ wɔyɛ saa.
